League of Nations New Budget 25

Stipulates Liaison Expenses for China

A Total of 450,000 Gold Francs

(Geneva) The budget for the International League of Nations for 1935 stipulates expenses for liaison between the League of Nations and China, totaling 450,000 gold francs. This expense includes technical health and other survey expenses in China for 1935, as well as the expenses required for technical cooperation between the League of Nations and China. The total amount of the League of Nations budget for 1935 is 30,461,300 gold francs, and its distribution and use include: 15,013,134 gold francs for the Secretariat, 8,536,046 gold francs for the International Labor Organization, 2,535,646 gold francs for the International Permanent Court, 114,984 gold francs for the Permanent Opium Committee, and 280,000 gold francs for the Nansen International Refugee Relief Bureau. In total, the League of Nations' budget expenditure for next year will be reduced by 366,500 gold francs compared to this year, i.e., 1934, and by 3,067,832 gold francs compared to 1933. (4th Havas)

Japanese Ambassador Ota Proposes to Russia to Withdraw Troops from the Border 26

Preliminary Exploration Nature, Russia's Attitude is Worth Noting

(Paris) Japanese Ambassador to Russia Ota visited Soviet Deputy Foreign Minister Stomonyakov (in charge of Far Eastern affairs) on the 31st of last month, explaining his personal opinion that in order to ease the situation in the Far East, the Japanese and Russian troops stationed on the Far Eastern border should be withdrawn immediately. The ambassador visited Stomonyakov again yesterday and suggested dismantling defensive fortifications. According to the Little Paris Daily, Ota's suggestion to the Soviet Russian government in his personal capacity is of great concern to foreign figures stationed in Moscow, as it is generally believed that Ota's visit is a preliminary exploration and a preparation for formal diplomatic negotiations. There is no doubt that this kind of proposal is extremely sensitive. If Russia rejects this proposal, Japan has an excuse to say that Russia refuses to try to ease the tense situation in the Far East. If Russia accepts this proposal, then the real beneficiary is Japan, because it is easy for Japan to withdraw its troops stationed in Manchuria. On the contrary, the defensive fortifications in Vladivostok and the coastal provinces are relied on by the Russian Red Army and cannot be easily abolished. The Little Paris Daily believes that it is difficult to determine at this time whether Ota's proposal can be accepted by Moscow. (4th Havas)

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Responds to Soviet Russian Protest 27

Arresting Employees Said to be False National Legal Rights

Night Trains Suspended on the Southern Section of the Middle East Railway

(Tokyo) Regarding the case of arresting Soviet employees of the Eastern Railway, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, at 7 pm on the 4th, received a written letter from Soviet Ambassador to Japan Yurenev to Foreign Minister Hirota on August 20. Therefore, Foreign Minister Hirota also replied to the Soviet ambassador in writing on September 4. The full text of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is as follows: Dear Sir, I have received your letter of August 22 regarding the case of arresting Soviet bureau members on the Eastern Section of the Eastern Railway on August 13, 14, and 16. After investigation, in recent months, there have been repeated conspiracies to overturn military trains in various places on the Eastern Section of the railway. Therefore, "Manchukuo" exercised its judicial power, and its basis is nothing more than this. As for the aforementioned case of overturning trains, the Japanese Ministry of the Army has not published any statement. As you said, the Japanese government should not be responsible for the various news published in the Japanese newspapers. There is no need to discuss this. On the Soviet side, it is said that the overturned trains in this case were only the actions of the local rebels, and even made a big statement, saying that the case was deliberately delayed by the Japanese and Manchurian sides and used this means, etc. On the Japanese and Manchurian sides, who are responsible for the defense of "Manchukuo," may I ask why they attempted to overturn military trains on the Eastern Railway? As for the point that there was no robbery, it cannot be regarded as the action of ordinary rebels. This can prove that (omitted)... Regarding the overturning of military vehicles and other similar incidents that disrupt public order in North Manchuria, since this week, the majority of Soviet personnel have been arrested at any time. The Soviet government believes that this should have been dealt with long ago, but the recent arrest seems to be related to the suspension of negotiations on the Eastern Railway. It also believes that damaging railway operations infringes on the Soviet Union's rights under the Eastern Railway Treaty. We believe that your government's view is entirely a false accusation. Therefore, we must point out that this kind of judicial event is absolutely necessary to ensure railway transportation and maintain public order along the line. Even if negotiations on the Middle East Railway have not been suspended, it is of course possible to launch it. (omitted) In short, the Japanese government is very concerned about where the aforementioned conspiracy comes from. As for the derailment incident related to this case, its location is limited to the Eastern Section of the railway, and most of the damaged trains are transportation trains for military supplies, and the supplies have not been robbed, and the victims are mainly Japanese and Manchurian people, with no Soviet people being harmed. This is completely different from the situation of ordinary train damage. As for the detainees this time, all of them are Soviet employees of the Eastern Section of the Eastern Railway and have all participated in this illegal society that disrupts the public order of "Manchukuo" and plots irregularities. The instructions issued by the rebels to blow up the railway and the supply of explosives are all handled by the Soviet employees of the railway. According to this report and various other circumstances, it seems that a part of the Soviet people have some connection with the plan in this case, and it can be said that this view is a natural trend. (4th Japanese United Telegram)

(Moscow) A telegram from Harbin stated that the Middle East Railway Administration had inquired with the Chief of Staff of the Railway Protection Army about the safety situation of the railway's southern section, but the headquarters of the Railway Protection Army did not respond. Subsequently, the Director of the Railway Administration, Rodi, ordered the suspension of night trains on the southern section. According to news from Bo Li, the Harbin press is using the recent train robbery on the southern section of the Middle East Railway to carry out its new anti-Soviet rumors, falsely claiming that a Soviet train attendant is colluding with bandits. At the same time, when listing the names of those who were harmed during the bandit attack, they were silent about the temporary serious injury of the Soviet train attendant Trebupengko. The Japanese and Manchurian press are trying to use these rumors to instigate an anti-Soviet campaign among the Soviet railway workers of the Middle East Railway, strongly accusing them of being related to the bandits who robbed the train. (4th Tass)

The Japanese Cabinet's Naval Policy Opinions Have Reached a Consensus 29

Osumi Reports to the Japanese Emperor

(Tokyo) Regarding the fundamental policy of disarmament countermeasures, Foreign Minister Osumi explained the content to Finance Minister Fujii on the 4th and asked for understanding. Thus, the opinions of all relevant cabinet members have reached a consensus. Foreign Minister Osumi met with Foreign Minister Hirota after the cabinet meeting and mentioned that he had obtained the understanding of Army Minister Hayashi and Finance Minister Fujii, and after discussing the handling methods with each other, he consulted with Prime Minister Okada. The result was decided as follows:

(1) The fundamental policy of disarmament countermeasures is an extremely important issue, so before the cabinet decides, Foreign Minister Osumi should enter the palace to report to the Emperor to show prudence.

(2) At the cabinet meeting on the 7th of this month, the draft for the notification of the abolition of the Washington Naval Treaty and the instruction for convening preparatory negotiations for disarmament in October of this year must be decided by the cabinet.

(3) The draft for the notification of the abolition of the Washington Naval Treaty must be submitted to the Privy Council at an appropriate time for decision. (4th Japanese United Telegram)

Count Hijikata Enters Russia and Scolds the Japanese Capitalist Class 30

The Imperial Household Ministry is Very Dissatisfied

(Tokyo) In order to purify the nobility, the Imperial Household Ministry investigated the actual situation of the nobility. Count Hisatake Hijikata, who was traveling abroad, violated the regulations of the Imperial Household Ministry, the Metropolitan Police Department, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, entered the Soviet Russian country, and scolded the Japanese capitalist class and praised the red literature at the Soviet Writers' Congress in Moscow. After receiving this information, the Imperial Household Ministry was indignant at his imprudent attitude and began actively investigating the truth. After the truth is ascertained, decisive measures will be taken. According to the authorities regarding this issue, Count Hijikata's actions are currently being investigated by the judicial authorities. His entry into Russia was not authorized by the authorities, and his imprudent speech has caused the authorities to impose more severe penalties. (4th Japanese United Telegram)

(Moscow) The Soviet Writers' Congress closed here yesterday. The congress passed the organization of the Soviet Writers' Union, which has about 2,500 members, including more than 1,500 from the Russian Republic, 160 from Ukraine, and 100 each from Georgia and Belarus. There are also members from various states. Unrest in Cuba 33

Student and Worker Strikes and Demonstrations

⊙Havana: For several weeks, the Cuban capital has been in turmoil. Today, students and workers launched a 24-hour strike to protest the deaths of two young men on Saturday. The presidential guard discovered the two young men hiding weapons, intending to break into the presidential palace. When their plot was exposed, they failed to escape and were shot dead by the guards. Agitators exaggerated the incident, claiming the two men were martyrs who sacrificed themselves for Cuban freedom, and delivered speeches to workers in the streets and alleys, inciting students. Thus, a general strike suddenly erupted, catching the authorities completely unprepared. Transportation has been temporarily disrupted. However, troops were ordered to patrol all roads, and in a short time, the agitators scattered throughout the city were cleared. Several demonstrators were injured during the clashes. (3rd National Telegram)

Foreign Wars: The Relationship Between British Dominions and the Mother Country 34

Differing Views from All Sides

Neutrality is Legally Impossible

(London) Whether the British mainland would naturally involve the dominions in war if it went to war with a foreign power is a question on which opinions differ greatly. A speech by South African Prime Minister Hertzog on this matter has attracted considerable attention. Hertzog stated that if the British mainland went to war because of a treaty to which the dominions had not explicitly acceded, the dominions would not bear any responsibility. The Locarno Treaty was one such example. Conversely, according to the most reliable sources, the Liberal Party, which is about to form a cabinet in Canada, has explicitly declared, "When Britain goes to war, Canada goes to war." When Sir Maurice Hankey, a member of the Imperial Defence Committee, visited the capitals of the various colonies of the Empire to discuss defense, the issue of the relationship between the dominions and the mother country was particularly important. Responsible parties in London believe that sovereignty in the British Empire belongs to the British mainland. If the mainland goes to war and a part of the Empire declares neutrality, it is legally impossible. However, this is only a matter of principle. Whether the dominions must actively participate in any war that the British mainland is involved in, regardless of the circumstances, has not been explained in detail by the speakers. (Note: Sir Maurice Hankey, a member of the Imperial Defence Committee, went to Australia in early August to participate in the centenary of the establishment of the state of Victoria. He took the opportunity to visit the capitals of various dominions to consult on imperial defense. See the telegram of August 8.) (3rd Havas Telegram)

Italian Population Soars 43

Birth Rate Higher in Rural Areas than Cities

Success of National Policy

⊙Rome: According to official statistics released today, the Italian government's policy of reclaiming wasteland and promoting the nation's "go to the people" policy has been very effective. In the first six months of 1934, Italy's birth rate exceeded the death rate by 223,983 people, of which 34,453 belonged to large cities and the remaining 189,530 belonged to small towns and villages. In other words, the birth rate in large cities increased by just over six people per thousand, while the birth rate in rural areas increased by just over twelve people per thousand. (3rd National Telegram)

US-Russia Debt Negotiations 44

Disagreement on Credit Extension Terms

(Washington) According to sources obtained by the Associated Press today, the obstacle to US-Russia debt negotiations is the disagreement over the nature of future credit extensions from the United States to Soviet Russia. In recent negotiations between the two countries on the debt issue, there has been complete understanding on both sides. Russian sources here deny that there are any difficulties regarding the total amount of repayment. It is heard that the negotiations between Secretary of State Hull and Russian Ambassador Troyanovsky have made great progress, but there is still no agreement on the issue of future credit extensions. The American business community is paying close attention to these negotiations because once the debt is resolved, Soviet Russia can place orders in the United States. Currently, because Soviet Russia is on the list of debtor nations, it cannot enjoy credit extensions in the United States under the Johnson Act. (3rd National News Agency Telegram)

New Commander of the Salvation Army 46

68-Year-Old Evangeline Booth Elected

(London) Evangeline Booth, daughter of the founder of the Salvation Army, was elected today to succeed Higgins as Commander-in-Chief. Ms. Booth, nearly 70 years old, has devoted her entire life to the work of the Salvation Army. In her youth, she personally participated in humble work while serving the poor, and was soon known as the "White Angel." Ms. Booth later went from England to Canada to lead the work there for eight years, establishing many schools, hospitals, and libraries. In 1904, she was elected commander of the Salvation Army in the United States. In the United States, she founded more than 1,600 educational institutions, nursing homes, and worker shelters. There were also opponents of her election as Commander-in-Chief this time, claiming that she had too much secular念 in the United States and that she was already sixty-eight years old. (3rd National Telegram)

(London) The Salvation Army's High Council today appointed Evangeline Booth, daughter of the founder of the Salvation Army, as the new commander of the Salvation Army, replacing Higgins, who will retire due to old age on November 10. It has been eight years since the Booth family last held this position, and this is the first time that a woman has held this top position, a groundbreaking event in the Salvation Army. Eight years ago, when Higgins was elected, Ms. Booth was also one of the candidates. Ms. Booth has 40 years of service in the Salvation Army, and for the past 30 years, she has been the leader of the Salvation Army in the United States. Although she is now 69 years old, she swims every morning and takes long walks or drives in the afternoon, which is her usual routine. In 1898, during the Klondike gold rush, Ms. Booth led a Salvation Army nursing corps to rescue the injured. The High Council declared after the election today that Ms. Booth's election was a sign of Providence. The entire council expressed its admiration for Higgins's contributions and swore allegiance to the new commander. It also stated that the organization of the Salvation Army will remain the same. A total of five candidates were nominated by the High Council today, including another woman, the daughter of the late General Bramwell Booth, who is also the niece of the new commander, Ms. Evangeline Booth. When the new commander left the election hall, the crowd outside cheered. It is said that the vote count will not be released. The new commander's annual salary is 500 English pounds, which does not come from the Salvation Army's funds, but is allocated from a special trust fund established by the late General Booth Boothby. (3rd Reuters Telegram)

German Medical Scientist Discovers Tumor Germ 47

(Berlin) Dr. Behrle, of the Dalen National Medical Association, announced today that he has discovered a tumor germ. He said that he discovered the germ under a microscope. He cultured the germ and injected it into animals. Soon after, the animals showed signs of tumors. Then, he re-cultured the tumor germ in these animals. The reason he was unable to discover it earlier was that the germ nests were extremely close to red blood cells, and it was necessary to use "special injection and analysis" to see the germ. Tumors only develop in people with alkaline blood. The tumor germ goes through seven stages, the first four of which are present even in healthy people. (4th Reuters Telegram)

Radio Transmission of Images 51

Will Become a Common Scientific Weapon

Second Machine Installed on Peak of Brocken

(Berlin) Germany's second radio image transmission machine was installed today by the German postal department on the highest peak of the Brocken mountain. The machine receives light rays transmitted from Berlin and then strengthens its light power and relays it to other stations. The reason why the machine must be installed on the top of the Brocken mountain is that according to recent inventions, radio image transmission requires an extremely high location to be more effective. The German postal authorities, based on the experience of recent years of testing, believe that radio image transmission will soon become an extremely common and applied scientific weapon. (3rd National Telegram)

After the promulgation of these revised tax rates, the provincial and municipal governments should not increase any taxes or levies on goods with reduced or exempted export duties, in order to align with the central government's concern for the difficulties faced by merchants. Lin'an Suffers Drought Disaster, Requests Emergency Relief 98

(Hangzhou) Lin'an County is the most severely drought-stricken county in western Zhejiang. According to investigations, out of 120,000 mu in the entire county, 70,000 mu are paddy fields. Of these, 20,000 mu have not been planted, and 50,000 mu have been planted but have completely withered. The remaining 50,000 mu of dry land will yield only 20% of the harvest. All miscellaneous grains have withered due to the drought. The county's grain supply is only sufficient for one month. The county magistrate and six representatives of the public group went to the provincial government to petition for the allocation of 500,000 yuan in local government bonds to provide work relief with cash and to immediately distribute 50,000 yuan in cash for emergency relief. Zeng Jianying, the Director of Public Relations of the Provincial Government, received them on behalf of the chairman and forwarded their request for handling. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Public Telegram 99

Telegram from Changyuan to the Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper, requesting transmission to the Chairmen and Directors of various provincial and charity organizations:

Heaven has sent a severe calamity, and the River God is raging again. Waves surge and crash, breaching dikes and breaking defenses. The aftermath of the calamity of Guiyou (1933) has not yet subsided, and the devastation of Jiashu (this year) is reported again. After the pain subsides, we cannot bear to weep again for the sake of the people. We humbly report that the river water began to rise on the 10th of this month, and by the morning of the 12th, mountain floods arrived, compounded by autumn rains, suddenly reaching heights of over ten feet in an instant. The Nine Branch Road, Liaoqiang Village, Xiangli Zhang, and others on the west bank were breached successively on the same day. The turbulent waves followed the old course, and by the morning of the 14th, the old districts one, two, three, and five, as well as the eastern half of district four, were once again inundated, with depths ranging from six to seven feet, four to five feet, three to four feet, and two to three feet. No house was left standing, and the sound was like thunder, gunfire, and the roar of the sea. The county seat was fortunately in the center of the flood, and in one day and night, the surrounding area rose to a depth of four to five feet, soaking the cracks from previous years. If it were not for diligent care, the city would have been breached. Therefore, although this flood is less turbulent than last year's, the crops are food for the fish and shrimp, and the courtyards are full of pits and valleys, even more so than before. The cries of sorrow, the sound of water, the roars of beasts, and the calls of birds, with the long autumn waters and the sky above and below the hills, the autumn of Jiashu is no different from Guiyou. Alas, homes are empty, the fields are a watery realm, there are no reserves, and the poor die in ditches. This is what is meant by empty barns. Great inundations occur repeatedly, and plagues follow, increasing deaths. This is what is meant by an empty population. If the people do not survive, what is the use of taxes? If taxes are not collected, how can there be催科? This is what is meant by an empty treasury. Relief for the dead is insufficient, so there is no time to manage rites. The scholars are reduced to beggars. This is what is meant by empty schools. These are the four emptinesses. Years of great floods fill the sky with gloom. Even if we wait for the waters to recede, how long will life last? This is what is meant by exhausted land. Those who have fled have not returned, and their fate is unknown. Those who remain flee again, but there is no land. This is what is meant by exhausted talent. Dikes are blocked and built, and the great work is just being completed, but before three seasons have passed, the flood returns.抚字督科 is extinguished. This is what is meant by exhausted official power. These are the three exhaustiones.

Considering that Changyuan is located in Kuangpu, dividing fields in Dongbi, and has been established as a county for two thousand years, those who live there are guilty and suffer the wrath of heaven. But why should the wise men of the past suffer such hardship? We ask that those who hold power and those who govern the borders not sit idly by and watch the entire county be destroyed. Therefore, we dare to speak again before you, pleading for compassion and prompt relief, so that the coming years will be filled with your kindness and virtue. We express our gratitude, and the sound of our voices is hoarse. We cannot bear the urgent pressure of hunger and cold.

Heng Xun, County Magistrate of Changyuan and Chairman of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee. Sun Tingrui and Mu Xiangzhong, Vice Chairmen. Yang Shulin, Representative of Disaster Victims residing in the province. Zhang Qin, Director of the Education Bureau. Cui Haixiu, Director of the Finance Bureau. Wang Lu, Director of the Construction Bureau.

The Distant East Cloaked in War Clouds (Correspondence from Harbin) 101

= Japan Actively Preparing =

= Soviet Union Standing Ready =

Since Japan occupied our four northeastern provinces, it has had two very clear military objectives. One is to take advantage of the situation and advance north, incorporating the area east of Lake Baikal into its territory, thereby gaining access to the oil in the northern part of Sakhalin Island and the benefits of the Siberian forests. The other is to take advantage of the victory and advance south and west, seizing the origins of wool and cotton production to serve as the base for its light industry. Previously, it did not know how much military force would be required to advance south and west, or how much money it would cost, so it did not dare to act lightly. Now that it has occupied Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe for nearly three years, it has a clearer understanding of the military realities, realizing that entering the pass is not very difficult, and advancing west is also very easy. This would not require much military force but would yield substantial benefits. Therefore, in terms of advancing south and west, it is not paying much attention to military deployments, only preparing some strength to cope with contingencies.

However, it is very active in terms of advancing north, because Japan needs to prepare for naval warfare in the Pacific, so oil is particularly important. It wants to use its army to seize oil resources in one fell swoop, so it has to make particularly intensive military deployments in northern Manchuria. First, along the Greater Khingan Mountains, it has built steel-reinforced concrete fortresses using cement and concrete. Many mountains with sparse human habitation are guarded by sentries, and hunting is prohibited. At the same time, the railway from Japan, crossing the sea from Tsuruga to Chongjin, crossing the Korean border, crossing the Tumen River, and reaching Changchun, has been completed. The railways from Changchun to Tao'an, from Huaiyuan to Solun, and from Erzhan to Heihe in Heilongjiang will probably also be completed after the autumn of this year. These are all military preparations. In addition, there is also the construction of automobile roads. The roads that have already been completed are over 2,500 kilometers long, and they are all spread out towards the northern border.

The construction of the Japanese air force, taking into account the four northeastern provinces, has more than fifty airfields. Almost forty of them are north of Liaoning, and the rest are scattered in southwestern Liaoning and the Rehe area.

Within the northeastern territory, there are five entire Japanese divisions, as well as special forces, cavalry, artillery, flying squadrons, tank squadrons, etc., totaling no less than 130,000 troops. In addition, there are two brigades of White Russian troops, 110,000 puppet troops, about 400 aircraft, and one tank regiment, and most of them are concentrated along the Chinese Eastern Railway.

In view of this threat, the Soviet Union will certainly not allow itself to be defenseless. So, the first step is to build defensive artillery forts and construct permanent trenches along the Heilongjiang and Ussuri rivers to cope with the above-mentioned military threats. At the same time, it is even clearer that the inconvenient transportation east of the Ural Mountains makes it difficult to concentrate huge forces and to transport supplies. This was the biggest factor in Russia's losses in the Russo-Japanese War. Now the Soviet authorities are well aware of this point, so the construction of a double-track railway alongside the Siberian Railway has already begun, and it should be completed in about a year.

Currently, the Soviet Union is gathering the Nineteenth Assault Army Corps in the vicinity of Vladivostok and Nikolayevsk. It includes eight

The opening price for British-American exchange was 5.005, up 1.75 from the closing price of British-American exchange on Saturday. American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market this morning, the pound was stable. The opening price for American-British exchange was 5.01, up 2.25 from the last closing price. Cotton and Wheat 105

New York Cotton: The New York cotton market opened lower by 5 points, mainly due to the textile industry's labor strike and the trend of foreign countries using other cottons to replace American cotton. The market situation stabilized before noon, rising 5 points at 10:30, but falling back by 1 point at 10:40.

Chicago Wheat: The wheat market opened at a price of 1.5 to 1.375 points lower due to retail sales. The textile industry strike also had a disturbing impact. Recent prices have risen by 1.25 to 2.5 points.

Liverpool Cotton: In the Liverpool cotton market, the price for the October contract was 6.86, up 1 point from yesterday's closing price.

Securities 107

It was predicted that demand would pick up somewhat within the month, facilitating a turnaround in the autumn. Factors unfavorable to the market included the anticipation that industrial activity across various sectors would continue to decline this week due to holiday closures. When the stock market opened this morning, market conditions were loose, and the prices of various stocks mostly declined slightly. Hopes for an early recovery in commerce have been extinguished by the textile industry strike. Therefore, the market appears to remain lackluster and uncertain. Promotion of Shanghai and Hong Kong National Goods and Industrial Products in Southeast Asia 108

Representatives Bring Samples for Exhibition at the Singapore Chamber of Commerce

Singapore Special Correspondent: Mr. Ma Yanzhang, a national goods promoter dispatched by the Shanghai industrial sector, accompanied by an American Mr. Erbo, carrying letters of introduction from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association, the Hong Kong Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, and the Manila Chinese Chamber of Commerce of the Philippines, arrived in the south on the President Polk. They arrived here from the Philippines yesterday morning and stayed at the Myriad Hotel. After arriving, the two gentlemen immediately visited the local Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, claiming that this trip was to represent Chinese national goods manufacturers in Shanghai to promote national goods in Southeast Asia, and brought seven large boxes of Chinese industrial products, totaling more than 200 kinds of samples, intending to exhibit them in various parts of Southeast Asia and engage in promotion. It is said that their trip to the south started on July 25 in Shanghai. They first went to Hong Kong, where they received enthusiastic support from Mr. Ma Wenhui of the Sincere Company, who also helped to collect more than 70 kinds of samples of products from Chinese factories in Hong Kong, which were also brought south. Therefore, the more than 200 kinds of samples brought by the two gentlemen this time represent the products of 97 Hong Kong and Shanghai national goods factories. The main products, such as silk fabrics, cotton fabrics, cosmetics, canned food, toys, shoes, socks, hats, light bulbs, electric fans, raincoats, medicines, lacquerware, tennis rackets, leather suitcases, curtain cloth, door curtain cloth, and other daily necessities, are all of excellent quality and rarely seen here. Mr. Ma and Mr. He held a reception for newspaper reporters at the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating their intentions, saying that China's national goods industry has developed extremely rapidly in recent years due to the influence of expensive gold and cheap silver, but most of them are still in the budding stage and have not yet been able to produce on a large scale, and lack the ability to directly promote them abroad. American businessman Mr. Spike founded a Chinese industrial product export company, specializing in acting as an agent for the export and promotion of various industrial products in China. Since its establishment, the company has been highly reputable and highly praised by national goods merchants in major domestic ports. Recently, in view of the fact that overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia are very happy to use national goods, but due to the lack of publicity and the lack of intermediary agencies to introduce them, the excellent products produced by Chinese manufacturers have not been noticed by overseas Chinese, and it is not easy for foreigners to recognize them, making the world's great market a place for Japanese goods to gallop, which is very regrettable. The purpose of our trip to the south is to introduce and promote the excellence of our Chinese products and do our best to promote them. Mr. Ma also said that this trip was originally from Shanghai to Hong Kong by Mr. Shi Xianchen and others. Later, Mr. Shi and others returned to Shanghai due to business, and he accompanied Mr. He from Hong Kong to the Philippines. In Manila, Philippines, he exhibited the samples he brought for many days and engaged in promotion. Everywhere he went, he was enthusiastically welcomed by the Chinese businessmen, and after visiting, they ordered goods from him one after another, and the number of letters from the company to the factories in Shanghai and Hong Kong to purchase them was very large. It can be seen that the overseas Chinese love to use national goods. Mr. Ma and Mr. He plan to stay in Singapore for a few days, and are scheduled to publicly display the more than 200 kinds of samples they brought at the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce starting on August 28. After the exhibition in Singapore, they will take the road to Penang, and then to Bangkok, Siam, and then to Calcutta, India, and Batavia and Surabaya in the Dutch East Indies, and to other parts of Southeast Asia. It is estimated that the trip will take three months, and they will be able to return to Shanghai around November of this year. (August 27)

The Three Route Army Captures Yiqian 109

—The City of Shicheng County Will Be Captured Soon—

—The Red Bandits of Ningdu Are Surrounded—

Nanchang Correspondence: When the Red Bandits broke through from the border of Fujian and Jiangxi to disturb the Minjiang River and invade eastern Fujian, a part of the Pseudo Third Army Corps Peng Dehuai and the Pseudo Fifth Army Corps Dong Zhentang were distributed in Shicheng, Ningdu, and Xingguo. The Pseudo Central Directly Subordinate Troops of Ye Jianying were holding on north of Huichang Yunmenling. The bandit troops of the Pseudo First Army Corps Lin Biao and others were scattered in the area of Changting and Ninghua in western Fujian, containing the East Route Army attacking Tingzhou, and another group of bandits from the Pseudo Seventh and Ninth Army Corps Fang Zhimin and Luo Binghui sneaked eastward, hoping to attack the unprepared National Army. Regarding the Sixth Division of the Pseudo Third Army Corps, which was holding on to Xingguo, it was repeatedly repelled by Zhou Hunyuan and reached Gaoxingxu. There are no major battles with the bandits guarding Ningdu because they are not the main force. A part of the Pseudo 35th Army Corps, which stubbornly defended Shicheng, was repeatedly attacked by the National Army, which was 口⼝⼝ advancing step by step, in the area south of Baishui and Xueheling. The Red Bandits seized Yiqian, which is located at the junction of Shicheng, Jiangxi, eastern Jiangxi, southern Jiangxi, western Fujian, and northern Fujian, and is essential for both military and economic reasons. Zhu Mao once sent a large number of bandits to garrison there, and transferred two to three thousand farmers, young and old, from 寗瑞　Hui to gather in Huangshimen to supplement the bandit army and drive them to withstand the artillery fire. Starting on the 28th of last month, the National Army launched an attack on various routes and occupied the bandit positions. In another battle until 1:00 PM, the key points of Nanlingnao and Huangtumen north of Yiqian were also captured by the central route. The regiment commander of the Pseudo Fourth Division and the battalion commander of the third battalion of the regiment were killed in battle, and many bandit soldiers were killed or wounded. The bandit forces were unsustainable, and the National Army was encouraged to continue the attack, and completely recovered Yiqian on the 29th. The remnants of the bandits retreated completely to the vicinity of Shicheng County. It was found that Yiqian was the gateway to Shicheng and also the key to Ningdu. It is only tens of miles away from Shicheng County. Now that it is owned by the National Army, Shicheng is like something in a pocket, and the northern half of Ningdu protrudes between Guangchang and Yongfeng, and has long been surrounded. Its southern half protrudes south of Shicheng Xingguo. Now that the ⼝⼝ and other route armies have captured Shixing, they have been very successful. If these two counties are captured, the bandits in Ningdu will have nowhere to go if they do not escape. (September 2)

The Organizational Outline of the Xikang Province Establishment Committee is Determined 110

Five to Seven Members with Two Divisions Underneath

Directly Under the Executive Yuan and Not Under the Command of Sichuan Province

Kangding Correspondence: After Huang Musong suggested that the central government set up a provincial government in Xikang, the relevant agencies such as the General Staff Headquarters and the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission discussed the matter. As a result, it was proposed to first establish a "Xikang Political Affairs Committee" to prepare for the establishment. After the province meets all the conditions for establishing a province, the provincial government will be formally organized. After the meeting was submitted to the central government for review, it was decided to change it to the "Xikang Province Establishment Committee," and ordered the Ministry of the Interior and the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission to draft an organizational outline and submit it for approval and implementation. Now that the ministry has been ordered, it has consulted many times, and the general decision is that (1) the name of the Xikang Province Establishment Committee is agreed; (2) it should be directly under the Executive Yuan and should not be under the command of the Sichuan Provincial Government and the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense Commissioner's Office; (3) there should be five to seven members of the committee, and one chairman; (4) there should be two divisions, a secretariat and a political affairs division, with several sections inside, and specialists should be hired to organize a design committee, or, in order to save public funds, several sections should be temporarily set up. The above principles, after repeated consultations, will be finalized, and a general outline will be prepared and submitted to the central government for implementation. According to a senior official who participated in the review, the organization should be smaller than the current provincial organization during the preparation period. After a considerable period of preparation, the small government will be formally organized and the committee will be abolished. Now the opinions of the central and local governments are unified, and this organization can be realized. (Xinmin News Agency)

The Red Bandit Fang Zhimin Flees to the Border Between Fujian and Zhejiang 111

Qingyuan and Zhenghe Counties are Ravaged by Bandits

Eastern Fujian Loses Approximately Four to Five Million Yuan

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the Red Bandit Fang Zhimin's forces failed to attack the provincial capital, they fled from Fu'an to Shouning, and then captured Xietan Town, the most prosperous town in the county. Later, after the 口⼝⼝ Division chased from Fu'an, and the 口⼝ Division stationed in Shoucheng joined forces to attack from the front and rear, the bandit forces were unsustainable and fled in different directions. One force fled through Xixi into Qingyuan County in Zhejiang Province, and the other force fled through Nanxi to Zhenghe County in northern Fujian. Yesterday, the provincial government has telegraphed the 口 Division to encircle and suppress the scattered bandits immediately to prevent them from penetrating deep into the inland of northern Fujian, and ordered the 口 Brigade to deploy defenses closely on the border between Fujian and Zhejiang.

Among the counties in eastern Fujian, the most heavily damaged by the bandits this time are Muyang and Baishi in Fu'an, Xietan in Shouning, and Xiamen in Fuding. Muyang and Xietan were robbed empty, and Baishi and Xiamen were burned to the ground. The total loss is estimated to be between four and five million yuan. Although the bandits have retreated, the people have no homes to return to and have sent representatives to the province to request relief. (1st)

Floods in the Dongjiang River in Eastern Guangdong Cause Dikes to Collapse in Various Counties 112

Refugees are Everywhere, and Crops are Completely Lost

Guangzhou Correspondence: The downstream of the Dongjiang River in Guangdong Province has been hit by a major flood. The first to bear the brunt is Huiyang County. When the Hui River receded, the flood spread to Boluo and Dongguan counties. Dozens of villages in Boluo along the Jiangsu River became a lake on the 23rd. The area around Weilu Lake in the county, which is connected to Sucun, is close to the Jiangbin River and has dikes as barriers. However, on the 26th of the month, the Dongliao River rushed down, and the dikes suddenly became dangerous. The villagers were unable to rescue them, and the entire dike collapsed at 3:00 AM that morning. Inside the dike, there are 18 villages and 26 districts, all of which became a huge flood. No less than thousands of houses collapsed in each village one after another. The villagers, supporting the old and carrying the young, fled to the plateau for refuge. The fields and gardens in Longxi and Longhua were also flooded, and more than one million yuan was lost in crops, property, and livestock in more than ten villages.

Dongguan County is the key point where the Dongjiang River flows into the Pearl River and exits the sea. The terrain is even lower than Boluo, so the area affected by the disaster this time is even wider. In addition to the tragic situation of the breach of the Shangdong Township base dike, which has been reported in the newspaper, the dikes in the first, second, and third districts have also repeatedly reported breaches recently. In the third district, the populations of Duzhou Township, Shuibei Township, and more than ten villages such as Xia Nan Huangjia are all farmers, who are engaged in agriculture. Because the land is close to the Dongjiang River, it has been repeatedly affected by floods and has suffered frequent crop failures. They have borrowed tens of thousands of yuan from the River Management Association to build the base gardens in various places. The project has just been completed, and a major flood suddenly arrived in the late of this month. On the night of the 23rd of the month, the dikes in Chikan Huangjia and Shuibei townships were breached by dozens of feet. There were more than ten breaches in total. The flood flowed into the third district, and the fish ponds, mulberry gardens, and rice fields in each village were submerged. It was midnight, and the villagers were awakened from their dreams. Unable to escape in time, many people drowned. At this moment, refugees are everywhere, with nowhere to live. Cries can be heard from time to time in the mountains and fields. On August 28th and 29th, the flood still had not receded, and Fulong Garden in the county was also in danger.

Shilong Town is a major station on the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway, where merchants gather and the market is prosperous. Since the late of August, the Lu Garden east road Sanatorium to the west, until the Baihua Road Zhongshan Road were flooded, the water was waist-deep, and the low-lying alleys were even more submerged. Large and small shops moved to trade in other places, and the station's terrain was higher, and the nearby area has become a temporary market. Residents in the city row boats to buy goods, and transportation is extremely inconvenient. This time the whole county was flooded, and in addition to rice, peanuts lost about more than ten thousand yuan in value. Other losses such as sugar cane, green麻菓 wood, and other items are also not small, truly a major catastrophe in recent years. (August 31)

Bengbu is Preparing to Establish the Fenghuai Local Court 113

The Court Site is Determined to Be in the Nija Garden

The High Court Sends Personnel to Prepare in the City

Bengbu Correspondence: The Anhui High Court, considering that Bengbu is the hub of the Pingpu Railway and the only major port on land in Anhui Province, only twenty or thirty miles away from Fengyang and Huaiyuan counties, plans to jointly establish the Fengyang Huaiyuan Local Court to handle civil and criminal lawsuits. After the High Court submitted the plan to the Judicial Yuan, it was delayed until now because there were no construction funds available. The provincial government has just raised more than 20,000 yuan. The High Court specially appointed Hu Shu as the director of the preparation committee, and led the preparation committee members Wu Fanghan and others to the city to set up an office to prepare. The Nija Garden on Guofu Street has now been designated, and surveying and mapping are underway. After the approval is obtained from the local authorities, bids will be invited and construction will begin, probably after October. It is reported that in addition to the court, a detention center will also be attached, which is expected to be completed in its entirety in February or March of next spring. After that, judicial affairs in Feng and Huai counties will be handled by the court, and the monthly operating expenses of the court will be allocated from the judicial fees of Feng and Huai counties, and the surplus funds from the recently abolished Shou County Local Court. (September 1, letter from Bing, a correspondent student of this newspaper)

Songjiang

Citizens in Southern Pu Report a Case of Corruption in Land Tax 114

Yang Leibo, Zhang Chengzhe, Zhuang Likang, Chen Zhengxian, Weng Xiding, and other citizens in Southern Pu, Songjiang County, sent telegrams to Chiang, the military commissioner of the Nanchang Camp, Yu, the standing committee member of the Central Party Headquarters and the president of the Court of Censors, Kong, the minister of finance, and Wang, the minister of education, stating that the coastal villages of this county have poor soil quality and very little harvest, and have never had land tax. Since the order to increase grain transport in the 18th year of the Republic of China, the owners have been unable to pay and have filed petitions for deferral. Those who were forced to pay grain transport by the village police and map officials were not a few. In September of last year, County Governor Jin Tiangang convened a meeting of more than ten owners' representatives, at which Che Zhao, the chief of the finance section, proposed to increase grain transport on the converted fields in Southern Pu and reduce and exempt all taxes by 60%, effectively collecting 40%. For the 22nd year, the 18th year was forcibly levied in order to alleviate the people's difficulties. This was approved by County Governor Jin in conjunction with Shen Zhengshu, a member of the Old Tax Clearing Committee, and submitted to the Provincial Department of Finance, which ordered Ye Zongcheng, the director of the First Land Tax Collection Office, to comply. Unexpectedly, the benevolence of the provincial government in reducing and exempting taxes has opened up the loopholes for those to hide and deceive. It was found that the increase in grain transport in Southern Pu was only more than 7,000 dan, but County Governor Jin actually included part of Northern Pu in it and reported more than 10,000 dan. The 3,260 dan of increased grain transport in Northern Pu were paid off by the owners year by year, and even in Southern Pu, some were forced to pay, but County Governor Jin actually hid the tax money and reported that there was no income for four years since the 18th year. To the superiors, he has reduced and exempted more than 10,000 dan of grain transport in the 18th, 19th, 20th, and 21st years, but to the subordinates, he did not recall the grain transport prints and strings that had been increased over the years. Can the procedures for handling land tax be like this? Moreover, at the beginning of the increase in grain transport in the converted fields, the books were compiled and the collection books were created, indicating the amount of Southern Pu and the amount of Northern Pu. A check of the files would make it clear. Section Chief Che was the section chief in the Finance Bureau during the tenure of She and two Shen, and was familiar with the finances of this county. How could he claim to be unaware? When the case was discovered and could not be remedied, he put Director Ye in custody and submitted a request to the Department of Finance to correct that the Northern Pu portion was not within the scope of reduction and exemption. His intention to embezzle was obvious. Moreover, the book was created and the strings were issued in the 23rd year, after the order to reduce and exempt taxes was issued. The original increased grain transport should have been reduced to 40%, but in May of this year, County Governor Jin still ordered the book writers to create the book and issue the strings as before, and the seals were ready to be issued. The citizen Xu Shilin and others found the land tax notice for the 23rd year and filed a complaint with the Department of Finance. When County Governor Jin heard about it, he reported to the Department of Finance that it had been stolen. His attempt to cover it up was obvious. In short, after the Finance Bureau was abolished, the county government was actually the competent authority for the county's finances. If there is no corruption in land tax, the county governor and section chief cannot be excused. If the blame is only placed on the collection director alone, how can it be fair? Leibo and others live along the coast. Since the conversion of fields to increase grain transport, they have suffered unbearably. They have repeatedly called for help and exhausted their voices, and finally won the approval of the Department to reduce and exempt taxes. Unexpectedly, the reduction and exemption of taxes has created an opportunity for County Governor Jin, Section Chief Che, Director Ye, and others to make a fortune. In total, the tax money from the increase in grain transport in the converted fields that they have embezzled is no less than 100,000 yuan. If this is not punished, where is the national law? Although County Governor Jin was once the secretary-general of the provincial government and has considerable influence with the province, the laws of the Republic of China strictly prohibit corruption. He is specially requesting your judgment to quickly investigate and punish him as a warning, which would be a great kindness.

The Songhang Liquidation Office Closes 115

After the Songjiang Bank went bankrupt due to the absconding of the president, it owed a considerable amount of public and private funds. Later, the county court designated accountants such as Xia Sunhuan to carry out the liquidation and organized a liquidation office. Lawyer Zhang Yuanmei acted as an agent to separately urge the debtors to pay, and the money recovered was distributed to the creditors at 17%. The rest has not yet been closed. After a long period of time, a part of the debt status was requested by the court to allow the liquidation office to be revoked, and the unfinished work was transferred to the directors and supervisors of the bank to be responsible for the liquidation. Now, Xu Shousheng, a representative of the creditors, has written to the liquidation office to inquire about the work that should be reported to all sectors of society since the liquidation office was completed. There are also mortgage credit debtors and the amount of debts that have not been sued, as well as the names and amounts of each household that is still being sued but has not yet been completed, and the amount of money that has been recovered. The liquidation office hopes to announce the liquidation office's calculation, in order to make a great faith, and to督促 the directors and supervisors to be responsible for the liquidation in the future. At this moment, the liquidation office is in the process of closing down, and it will definitely be able to reassure all sectors of society regarding the above request.

Yang Jie and Liu Wendao Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 126

=Liu States that World War Is Not Likely to Occur in the Short Term=

=Yang Will Go to Jiangxi to Meet Jiang Within Days and Offer Suggestions=

=Mayor Wu Gave a Banquet for Liu Last Night; He Will Go to the Capital Today=

Yang Jie, President of the Army University, and Liu Wendao, China's Minister to Italy, the special envoys sent by the central government to Europe to study military affairs, returned to Shanghai yesterday afternoon on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso. Mr. Liu is scheduled to go to Nanjing today and then to Jiangxi to meet with Wang and Jiang, and then return to his ancestral home in Wuxue to take care of his grandmother's funeral. He will return to Europe on an Italian ship next month. Yang plans to rest briefly in Shanghai before going to Jiangxi to meet with Jiang and report on the situation. The details are as follows:

Arrival in Shanghai 127

Mr. Yang and Mr. Liu returned to China on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso. The ship entered the Wusongkou around 10 AM yesterday and docked at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong at 11:30 AM. The welcoming party crossed the river to board the ship. The two gentlemen disembarked and transferred to the Jianghai Customs Jinghai small steamer to cross the river to Pudong. At 12:20 PM, they landed at the new customs wharf and went to their residences to rest. Tang Hanzong, an electrical chemistry and electrometallurgy engineer from the University of Grenoble in France, also returned to China on the same ship yesterday.

Welcoming Personnel 128

Yesterday afternoon, those who went to the ship to welcome them included He Yaotsu of the Military Affairs Commission, Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau, Wang Zemin, Dean of Education of the Army University, Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Geng Jiaji, Secretary of the Municipal Government, Zhang Mengling, representative of the Foreign Affairs Office, Mei Zhu, Wu Danzhen, Wang Picheng, Shi Guofan, officials and staff of the Army University, Italian Minister to China Bauscari, Du Yuesheng, Mrs. Yang, Mrs. Liu and many other relatives and friends, who boarded the small steamers of the Public Security Bureau and the Junpu Bureau, went to the wharf to welcome them.

Yang's Remarks 129

According to Yang Jie's remarks to reporters, he was ordered by the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission in November last year to go abroad to Europe with five members to study the military education and military facilities of various countries. Except for the five members who had returned to China earlier, he arrived in Shanghai today. During the inspection in Europe, he visited about twenty countries, and the situation was very good. The facilities of the armies of various countries are very modern, and the results obtained are quite numerous. However, because it involves military secrets, the results cannot be arbitrarily published. The materials obtained from this inspection are quite numerous and have been sent to Chairman Chiang at any time. Various countries are actively expanding their military equipment, and their morale is also very strong. However, the internal situation in various countries is unstable. Various countries have their own strengths in military technology, some focusing on the army, some focusing on the air force or navy, depending on the environment and terrain of their countries. However, they all devote their full efforts to strengthen their national defense, which is the same trend. He is scheduled to go to Lu in the next few days to meet with Chairman Chiang, report on the inspection process, and offer suggestions.

Liu's Remarks 130

According to Wendao, his leave of absence to return home is to build a tomb for his grandmother and to report the latest international situation to the central government, with no other tasks. The vacation is a total of three months. After spending two months on the round trip, he will stay in the country for about one month and then return to his post on the Conte Rosso. Although various European countries are currently actively expanding their military equipment, according to his observation, there will definitely be no war in the next five years. Although the atmosphere between Japan and Russia is very tense, it has eased due to the peace in Europe, and there will be no conflict for the time being. Although the European situation has eased slightly due to Germany's concessions, we must never think we are fortunate, because the contradictions and struggles between countries are becoming increasingly acute. We should bury ourselves in preparation to prevent the future. He decided to go to Nanjing tomorrow (that is, today) to meet with Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, and then go to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang and report everything. After staying in Lu for a short time, he will go to his ancestral home in Wuxue to build a tomb for his grandmother and return to Europe next month on the Conte Rosso.

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng personally visited the residences of Mr. Yang and Mr. Liu around 4 PM yesterday. Mr. Wu also hosted a banquet at Xinghualou on Fourth Horse Road at 8 PM last night to welcome the two gentlemen, accompanied by Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau, and other dignitaries. =A Vicious Assault Occurred in Moji=

=Today They Will Petition Party and Government Agencies=

More than 80 overseas Chinese in Japan were suddenly squeezed out by Japan and unreasonably expelled to return to China. They arrived in Shanghai at 10 AM yesterday on the Japanese mail ship Kasado Maru. When the ship arrived in Moji, 31 overseas Chinese were forced to disembark and wait for other ships to return home. A vicious assault also occurred at that time. Therefore, those who arrived in Shanghai yesterday included 50 men and women, scheduled to petition the party and government agencies today. The details are as follows:

Arrival in Shanghai Yesterday: A Wretched Sight 138

The Kasado Maru entered the port at 9 AM yesterday and docked at the Xinhuishan Wharf in Pudong at 10:30 AM. Liu, a member of the foreign affairs section of the first section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Xia Zhongming, a member of the second section, and Inspector Zhou all arrived at the port to receive them and take care of everything on their behalf. The overseas Chinese were all wearing Western suits, each with a red silk scarf on the left lapel, with the words "Overseas Chinese in Japan" written on it. The women were wearing ordinary casual clothes. Because everyone was overly stimulated and exhausted from the journey, they were quite listless and looked extremely wretched. After the overseas Chinese arrived in Shanghai, they temporarily stayed at the Daxin Public Inn in the 16th district. The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission also sent Tan Zhonglu and Li Zhujian to the hotel to express their condolences.

The Expulsion Process Is Outrageous 139

The Xin Xin News reporter interviewed Chen Fengqing, the representative of the expelled overseas Chinese, on the ship. According to him, a total of 81 men and women were unreasonably expelled by Japan. They were all from Yongjia and other counties in Zhejiang and had been doing business in Japan for many years. Most of them had established families and lived in Niigata, Yamagata, and other prefectures in Japan. Among them, most were engaged in the restaurant business and were all peaceful and law-abiding citizens. In recent years, the Kuomintang's party affairs have developed significantly abroad, so they also organized the Kuomintang's direct branch in Sendai. Overseas Chinese joined as party members very enthusiastically, which was discriminated against by the Japanese. This time, the Japanese authorities unreasonably expelled overseas Chinese who had lived in Japan for many years and had always been law-abiding, which was beyond our expectations. What is most hateful and outrageous is that the expelled overseas Chinese workers, except for carrying their personal clothing, were not allowed to take any other items. All the movable items and properties accumulated by the overseas Chinese businessmen through years of hard work and thrift were unreasonably confiscated. When they were expelled, they asked the consulate to negotiate with them, but the authorities also said that the Japanese were barbaric and unreasonable, and it was impossible to reason with them. They planned to report to the government and make an overall negotiation with the Japanese side. They were temporarily unable to deal with the suffering of our people who were forced to suffer, so we could only endure the humiliation and return home and ask the authorities for assistance.

Forced Landing and Assaults on Overseas Chinese 140

After the ship departed from Yokohama, it was relatively peaceful along the way. Unexpectedly, when it arrived in Moji, the Japanese side, because a large number of overseas Chinese were expelled and returned to China, was afraid of being criticized by foreigners and the resentment of our compatriots. They did not hesitate to adopt a method of covering their ears and stealing the bell and specially sent more than 150 soldiers and police, most of whom were carrying weapons such as guns and clubs, with a fierce momentum, forcing the overseas Chinese to return to China in two batches. The overseas Chinese believed that since they had already been expelled, there was no need to return to China in any particular order and expressed their unwillingness to disembark, which angered the wild Japanese and implemented a military forced landing. The order was immediately disrupted, and the cries of wives and children were unbearable to hear. As a result, 31 people were forced to disembark and detained there, waiting for other ships to return home. At the time of the chaos, many overseas Chinese were injured, especially Zai Changtao, who was hit on the head, bleeding profusely. Zhou Yishun, Pan Rishun, Zhou Baozhen, and Wu Linhao were also seriously injured, and their lives are still unknown.

Petitions Today for Assistance 141

The overseas Chinese originally planned to petition the party and government agencies immediately after arriving in Shanghai yesterday. Later, because of the expulsion process and the re-assault along the way, they planned to write a memorial, asking for assistance, but there was not enough time, so they changed it to go to the Public Security Bureau for registration at 9 AM this morning, and then petition the party and other agencies in the city. They will immediately go to Nanjing to request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the Japanese government, and then return to their ancestral homes to find other livelihoods.

Presenting to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to Request Relief 142

After arriving in Shanghai, the overseas Chinese felt that there was no way to appeal and specially presented to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to request that it be presented to the central government for relief. The memorial reads as follows: The overseas Chinese in Japan originally operated small businesses in various parts of northeastern Japan and have always been extremely law-abiding. On August 10, they were suddenly expelled by Japanese officials. On August 14, all of them went to Wang Hongnian, our Consul General in Yokohama, to ask for accommodation. A total of 73 men and women arrived and stayed at the Chinese Guild Hall for two weeks. Our Consul General specially purchased ship tickets on their behalf, ordering them to return to China on the Kasado Maru. All 73 people left Yokohama at 11 AM on August 27. On the way through Nagoya, Osaka, and Kobe, they were forcibly inspected by the Japanese maritime police, subjected to violence, and beaten. Our overseas Chinese Zhou Baozhen was thrown into the sea by the Japanese army, but fortunately, he was rescued in time and did not drown. Wu Linhao was walking on the ship's building when he was beaten with a weapon by a Japanese policeman, and the wound on his forehead was three inches wide, and blood flowed all over the floor, fainting and losing consciousness for two hours. Other acts of violence are too numerous to mention. After arriving in Moji, the Kasado Maru was originally scheduled to depart at noon, but it was specially extended. At 7 PM that day, 190 Japanese maritime police came into the cabin and tied all the people with hemp ropes and took them ashore to the police station for interrogation. That night, three policemen were on duty, taking turns whipping them. Those who were too seriously injured died and revived. In addition, illegal torture was used, and many people were seriously injured. The sound of crying was incessant, and it was extremely cruel. Among the overseas Chinese, more than 30 people were detained elsewhere, and their lives and deaths are still unknown. Among the overseas Chinese, there were those who married Japanese women. The husband and wife came together, but the three Japanese women were suddenly detained by the Japanese police, and their families were separated, which made people's hair stand on end. Our overseas Chinese have always been law-abiding and have not committed any crimes. They have suffered this misfortune simply because of the decline of the country's power. Having suffered unemployment and torture, the human hell is almost the same. The ship departed on the 2nd. Zhou Baozhen was injured due to falling into the water and is currently being treated at the Moji Mail Ship Company. Wu Linhao was also injured in the head in Moji, and his life is in danger. In addition, 30 people are still detained in prison, and their lives and deaths are unpredictable. When the overseas Chinese left, they saw Pan Rishun and Zhou Yishun, who had fainted from the beating, and it was difficult to rescue them. Currently, the postal and telecommunications agencies in various parts of Moji are all controlled by the authorities, and there is no news. Our consul is also helpless. The overseas Chinese are spared the tiger's mouth and return to their homeland. The pain is immeasurable, and we ask the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to forward it to the central government for relief, and we will be very grateful.

The Expelled Overseas Chinese Return to Shanghai on the Kasado Maru (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Special Investigation Record of National Products Industry 150

(3) Cotton Knitted Underwear Industry

Cotton knitted underwear, including undershirts, underpants, and swimsuits, is a newly emerging industry. Initially, all of these were imported goods. In the past ten years or so, factories in this sector have gradually developed, reducing imports by 60-70%. This can be considered an achievement of national products factories. The reporter specially visited Mr. Ren Shigang, General Manager of Wuhe Weaving Factory, a leader in the cotton knitted underwear industry, and inquired in detail. He was kind enough to provide information on the general situation. The following is a special record:

There are dozens of businesses in the cotton knitted underwear industry, specializing in the manufacture of undershirts, underpants, and spring and autumn shirts. Five years ago, an industry dinner party was organized to connect emotions and maintain market prices. However, only fourteen companies joined. Prices for both winter and summer products are carefully studied and then set. The annual sales volume of these products is approximately 7-8 million yuan. Wuhe Factory alone has annual sales of over 1 million yuan. In the past two or three years, the number of companies in the industry has been increasing, most of which are small, family-run factories with capital of around 10,000 to 20,000 yuan. As a result, production is increasing and has become a trend of supply exceeding demand. Some companies specialize in the production of fabrics instead of clothing. These fabrics are sold to rubber factories as lining cloth or resold to sewing factories to make clothing. In recent years, rubber sales have declined, the market has been sluggish, and the environment has deteriorated, making sales even more difficult. At the same time, production is increasing, and prices are falling, which has led to a decline in the sales of these products. Regarding raw materials, domestic yarn can be used for the organization of thermal shirts, with 20-count, 16-count, 8-count, 7-count, and 6-count yarns being the most common. Undershirts of 42-count and below are all woven with domestic yarn. However, fine undershirts must be woven with 80-count to 100-count and 120-count yarns. For these raw materials, except for a small portion purchased from Chinese yarn factories, the rest must be purchased from the United Kingdom and the United States. Next, the working area was visited. From the entry of the yarn to the completion of the clothing, there are 24 working steps, and the procedures are extremely complicated, and sorting requires a lot of attention. Because the manufacturing is continuous, each part must be consistent and strive for scientific production methods in order to make the products exquisite and popular. The cleanliness and orderliness of Wuhe Factory meet scientific principles everywhere, so it can produce excellent products and sell them well in the market. As for sales, due to the recent decline in rural areas, the purchasing power of the general public is weak, and sales are quite difficult. It is not easy to lend money to all parties, and current sales are inevitable. At the same time, industry competition is fierce, discounts are falling frequently, and foreign goods are dumped to compete for the market, which is becoming more and more intense. Looking ahead, it is not possible to be optimistic. Among the companies in the industry, those with stable operations can barely maintain the status quo in recent years without failing. Mr. Ren believes that the future trend of our industry is: (1) the government should increase tariffs on similar foreign goods; (2) industries should maintain each other and not kill each other for meaningless sacrifices; (3) the whole country should work together to use national products; and (4) social leaders and intellectuals should do their best to promote and encourage, and lead by example. After this, the development of this industry may be unlimited. At present, Japanese goods are still the most common among imported goods, especially in North China. However, imported goods have been reduced in recent years in South China and Central China. However, the sorting work of imported goods is indeed excellent, and the cost is also low. If this industry wants to compete, it must save on floating expenses, work hard, and have absolute cooperation between labor and capital, and the financial sector must sincerely help. Mr. Ren also said that this factory feels that the current situation in rural areas is that it is difficult for this industry to develop temporarily, and he hopes that everyone will love national products, so that the purchasing power of all parties will increase, and the development of this industry can be expected. Mr. Ren is a Bachelor of Engineering from the University of Hong Kong. He has been starting a business in Shanghai for seven or eight years. He has contacted the industry to publicly set prices, which is trusted by all parties. Recently, he has established Chinese National Products Companies in various places and went to investigate without any effort, which is especially rare.

Gaogiao Rural Improvement Association Newsletter 151

Preparatory Meeting for the First General Meeting

The Shanghai Gaogiao Rural Improvement Association held its first preparatory meeting at the Local Association located at 138 Jing'an Temple Road at 5:00 PM the day before yesterday. The attendees were Zhang Chuanzheng, Pan Hongding, Zhong Yuliang, Shi Liangcai, Xie Bingchong, Zhao Dixian, Qu Shao Yi, Du Yuesheng, Gui Yanfang, Zou Bingwen, Huang Renzhi, Chen Zheqing, Guo Shun, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, Lü Yuequan, Liu Zhanen (represented by Wang Kuisheng), Wei (represented by Lai Douyan), and Ding Fengshan (Ding Rusong). Those attending as observers were Wang Kuisheng, the secretary, Liu Guofan, the secretary, and Lian Yousan. There were a total of thirty members, with twenty-one attending. After the bell rang to start the meeting, Mr. Du Yuesheng first gave an opening speech, stating in brief: "Esteemed members, today, as the convener, I would like to say a few words before the formal meeting begins. The urgent need for rural improvement in our country is evident from all perspectives and is worthy of our efforts. Although some may say that doing it only now is like applying medicine after the illness has worsened, or like trying to quench a distant fire, I believe that doing something is always better than doing nothing. As long as we work hard, regardless of the degree of success, we can at least find some comfort in our conscience towards the country and society, and we will surely gain some experience and understanding in the path of national self-salvation. The colleagues at the Local Association spent a long time investigating and researching, and finally selected the northern part of Gaogiao District and Gaoxing District in this city as the first experimental area, because it happens to be my hometown, so I was entrusted to take responsibility for initiating the organization. After two months of preparation, the permit from the Municipal Party Department has been issued, and the office will soon be moved to Gaogiao to start work. Today, I feel very happy and honored that so many comrades who are concerned about rural improvement have gathered together to hold the first grand preparatory meeting. Now, I would like to ask everyone to elect a temporary chairman to preside over today's proceedings." Later, the group unanimously elected Mr. Du as the temporary chairman, and first asked Mr. Shi Liangcai, the chairman of the Local Association, to report on the preparatory process and the procedures for registration. Mr. Huang Renzhi read out the organizational outline, which was amended and passed item by item. After that, Du Yuesheng was elected as the chairman of the association and the chairman of the board of directors. The chairman then proposed Ding Fengshan, Zhang Wei, Huang Renzhi, Liu Zhanen, Xie Bingheng, Zhong Yuliang, Su Shude, Yang Shuyu, Pan Hongding, Mu Ouchu, and Qu Shao Yi as eleven directors, and designated Ding Fengshan as the economic custodian. Mr. Liu is from Northeast China, graduated from a rural normal school, and served as the principal of Shenyang Dongling Elementary School and Tangshan Mining Area Elementary School, and also as the secretary of the Eryou Club. He is knowledgeable and experienced in rural education and represents the youth of Northeast China, which can remind the public not to forget to recover the Northeast territory. Mr. Lian Yousan founded a rural elementary school in Gaogiao and has nine years of struggle history. He is currently the principal of Rixin Elementary School and has always had a strong desire to improve the economic life of the countryside. It is especially commendable that he has obtained the permission of Mr. Xie Bingheng, the school director, to devote half of his time to serve as the secretary of the Rural Economic Department of the association. Finally, Secretary-General Wang Kuisheng briefly reported on the work schedule and the phased plan for the first year. After some discussion, the meeting adjourned. Some members gathered at Zhongshe for dinner and a lively discussion. Soon, they will move to that place to work. After the Du Ancestral Hall Hospital is completed, the office will officially work at the Jiqun Hospital.
