Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegrams Guangdong Finance Department Again: National Products Should Not Be Subject to Special Taxes 156

Within a Country, It is Valuable to Adjust Surpluses and Deficiencies

It is Inappropriate to Imitate the Behavior of Tariff Wars

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent another telegram to the Guangdong Finance Department yesterday regarding the special tax on national products in Guangdong Province, which stated: "To Guangzhou Guangdong Finance Department: Our chamber previously telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Guangdong Provincial Government regarding the proposal in Guangdong Province to establish a bureau to collect special taxes on imported foreign goods and goods entering from outside the province, requesting that national products be excluded from the scope of special taxes and handled separately, in order to protect domestic production. We received on August 29th Guangdong Provincial Government Approval No. 4335, which stated: 'We have received your telegram. It has been found that the Construction Department previously proposed collecting a special import tax on foreign goods in order to supplement the province's industry and commerce. This was submitted to the 288th meeting of the 6th Committee of this government, which decided to hand it over to the Finance Department for review and to draft specific measures for submission for approval. We have not yet received a reply. Regarding the previous situation mentioned in the telegram, please handle it in conjunction with the Finance Department.' We found that the approval mentioned the Construction Department's proposal to collect a special import tax on foreign goods, (omitted). However, the provincial government did not copy the Construction Department's original proposal, nor did it state in the approval. Our chamber has already explained the interests of this matter in detail in the Yang Telegram to the provincial government on August 7th. Since it has been forwarded for review, we believe that your department will consider it in detail. Our chamber believes that this matter is of great importance and has the following to add. It has been found that Guangdong Province has abundant products and has recently been determined to revitalize industry. For example, the rubber of Qiongzhou and the soda ash made in Guangdong are sold to other provinces, and the government has explicitly ordered that they be exempt from transit taxes. As for sugarcane, Shanghai and Qingdao sugar merchants have been reported to be placing orders in large quantities, as Guangdong Province has been striving to improve the quality. It is evident that within a country, it is valuable to adjust surpluses and deficiencies and exchange what one has for what one needs. It is inappropriate to divide regions like foreign countries and apply the behavior of European tariff wars to the same country. If each province has its own special products and suitable crafts, Guangdong Province should focus on the big picture and develop its strengths if it wants to remedy industry and commerce. It does not need to exclude products from other provinces, so that there is no place for development in Guangdong Province. Only then can it be said that it has done its best to support industry. Moreover, the state is exempting transit taxes on Guangdong Province's special products, which should be levied as a reward. However, Guangdong Province suddenly created a special tax after the abolition of likin, which has no legal basis and is used to resist goods from other provinces. In terms of law and reason, it is unforgivable. If this move is realized, it will be tantamount to treating Shanghai factories as outside the law and reducing national products to foreign goods, causing the immature industry that is fluttering in the wind and rain to fall into a narrow and unpromising field. The Shanghai merchants' interests are closely related, and public sentiment is indignant. How can we plan a method to deal with it? Guangdong Province's commerce and finance have many connections with other provinces. How can it transcend the mundane and not seek mutual assistance? This is using a spear to attack a shield, which is definitely not in Guangdong Province's interest. We will once again earnestly present the interests. We hope that your department will distinguish and handle it separately, which would be most fortunate. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce."

China Factory Inspection Association Held its Second Annual Meeting Yesterday 157

Requested the Central Government to Send Personnel to Various Countries for Observation

Requested to Convene a National Factory Inspection Conference

The China Factory Inspection Association held its second annual meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at Minqing Road in the city center. More than 20 members, including Cheng Qiyuan and Tian Heqing, attended. First, members from various regions reported on the general situation of factory inspection work in each district and the actual situation of factory disasters. Then, the following proposals were discussed: (1) The association's membership should be expanded. It was decided to divide the association's membership into three types: ordinary, basic, and sponsored. A: Anyone who is interested in factory inspection can join as an ordinary member. B: All graduates of the former Ministry of Industry's Factory Inspection Personnel Training Institute are basic members. C: Teachers, labor experts, and those interested in factory inspection at the former Ministry of Industry's Factory Inspection Personnel Training Institute may be invited by the association as sponsored members. (2) Farewell to Comrade Lu Jicang, a member of the association, who is going abroad for observation, and entrust Mr. Lu to observe the British factory inspection system. (3) Request the Ministry of Industry to convene a national factory inspection conference as soon as possible to facilitate the administration of factory inspection. (4) Request the central government to select current factory inspectors to go to various countries to observe factory inspection administration and other factory inspection technical work. (5) Issue a declaration to promote the administration of factory inspection in provinces and cities across the country. (6) Elect the executive committee members for this year. The elected members are Tian Heqing, Wang Ying, Cheng Qiyuan, Li Chongpu, Li Shude, Shen Risheng, Li Shikui, and seven others. (7) Decide on the location of the next annual meeting, which will be held in Wuxi, and recommend Mr. Cheng Qiyuan to prepare for the next annual meeting.

Division of Municipal and County Tooth Tax Implemented 158

Effective from September 1st

Shanghai's tooth tax is divided into long-term and short-term types. It has always been allocated by the Jiangsu Provincial Education Funds Management Office to supplement Jiangsu Province's education funds. However, the municipal government has repeatedly requested the Jiangsu Provincial Government to allocate the tooth tax in the urban area for municipal collection in order to clarify the boundaries. It is now known that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has approved the allocation and will implement it from September. It is also reported that after the municipal finance bureau receives the municipal tooth tax, it will send personnel to collect it and will not invite merchants to contract for it. As for the county area, the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office has ordered the Shanghai County Government to invite merchants to bid for contracting the short-term tooth tax, with a bid amount of 3,200 yuan, which is scheduled to be opened at the county government on the 11th of this month.

Cotton Traders Oppose Yarn Association's Cotton Inspection 159

We have already transferred the telegram to the government through the general assembly for presentation. According to Article 14 of the Cotton Prohibition Regulations, the effective date of these regulations shall be determined by decree. That is to say, even though the regulations have been promulgated, whether they are implemented remains to be assessed. However, the Shanghai Chinese Yarn Factory United Association actually published a notice in the newspaper yesterday stating that from September 1st, goods must be imported in accordance with the conversion stipulated in the Prohibition Regulations. This kind of illegal act is definitely not what our association can recognize. Moreover, it is worth the new flower market. If no measures are taken to stop it, it will endanger the national cotton industry. We intend to ask the general assembly to telegraph the government again to present it on our behalf, so as to avoid major disputes and improve the situation step by step." Shanghai-Pinghu Joint Transport Long-Distance Bus Robbed South of Caohejing

Two Thieves Disguised as Passengers, Two Thieves Ambushed Mid-Way

Police Received Report and Pursued, Killing One and Wounding One

Those Responsible for Local Public Security Should Pay Attention

The Shanghai-Pinghu joint transport long-distance bus, which was driving between Shanghai and Pinghu, was robbed by bandits south of Caohejing at about 10:30 AM yesterday. After the incident, the police officers of the Sixth District and Third Precinct pursued and killed one thief and wounded one thief north of Huiling Station. The details of the situation are recorded below:

Passenger Transformed into Robber 162

The Shanghai-Pinghu through bus service, jointly operated by the Shanghai-Minhang-Nantuo Bus Company and the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Administration, runs exclusively between Shanghai and Pinghu. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the No. 6 bus departed from Guohuo Road in Shanghai on schedule, carrying over twenty male and female passengers. When the bus arrived at the Tushanwan station, two additional male passengers boarded – one wearing a white short shirt and pants, the other wearing a silk long gown, a straw hat, and holding bus tickets to the Qianliangmiao station. Shortly after, the bus continued its journey. Unexpectedly, when it reached about one kilometer south of Caohejing, the two passengers who had boarded later suddenly produced handguns, threatening and coercing the passengers to hand over all their gold and silver jewelry, cash, and foreign currency. They also forced the driver, Zhang Lansheng, to stop the bus. The passengers looked at each other in dismay, unable to resist, and had to submit to the robbery. Simultaneously, two other bandits, who had been lying in ambush nearby, also joined in, boarding the bus to rob and plunder.

Hastily Fleeing with the Loot 163

Fortunately, at that moment, the No. 7 through bus, traveling from Pinghu to Shanghai, also arrived at the scene. Noticing the No. 6 bus stalled along the way, they assumed it was due to mechanical failure and stopped to inquire. Upon seeing this, the bandits, fearing exposure, hastily got off the bus and fled with the stolen goods. After the passengers explained what had happened, the bandits were already far away. The accompanying inspectors, Chen Jueyan and Shougen, arranged for the passengers from the No. 7 bus to transfer to the No. 6 bus. They then transported the robbed passengers to the sixth district, third precinct station in Caohejing to report the incident. Simultaneously, they reported the situation to the company and then returned to the scene of the crime, starting the No. 6 and No. 7 buses as usual.

Fierce Battle at Huiling Station 164

Upon receiving the report, the third precinct of the sixth district immediately dispatched a large number of armed police officers, riding in vehicles and bicycles, to search along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, Caohejing Station, and the Huiling Station area. Near the northern side of Huiling Station, they suddenly encountered two suspicious individuals walking hastily ahead. The police officers immediately rushed forward and ordered them to stop for inspection. Unexpectedly, the two men were the bus robbers. Seeing armed police officers chasing them from behind, they desperately opened fire on the police officers. As a result, the police officers returned fire, triggering a fierce battle at the northern side of Huiling Station. Bullets flew everywhere, like a string of pearls. After a brief standoff, the bandits were overpowered and retreated towards the Northwest Hongqiao Town, Baziqiao area, fighting as they went. When they reached Wangjia Lane, two more bandits joined the fight. However, one of the original bandits was shot in the leg. Another bandit dragged him up and carried him away as they fled. One bandit was shot in the chest by a police officer and fell to the ground on the spot. He was captured. Upon searching his person, the police found a jade bracelet, a jade ring, a gold-filled wristwatch, a gold pocket watch, a gold watch chain, and a six-inch handgun with the number 129012. He was taken to the precinct. Under interrogation, he identified himself as Zhang Shiying from Xujiahui and said nothing more. He soon died from his injuries. This morning, the court was notified to conduct an autopsy. The bureau was notified to dispatch detectives to pursue the remaining bandits, but they have not yet been apprehended.

Investigation of the Robbery 165

Regarding the robbery, subsequent investigation suggests that it may have been motivated by the excessive amount of gold and silver jewelry worn by the passengers. However, the fact that the bandits were lying in ambush in the middle of the journey suggests that it may have been pre-planned. Currently, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway sees heavy traffic of Chinese and foreign travelers. Moreover, the area south of Caohejing is a bustling district. The occurrence of a daytime bus robbery is indeed rare. It is hoped that those responsible for maintaining public order will take effective measures to address this, lest people view the area as a dangerous place. The names of the robbed passengers are listed below: (1) Liu Cui, from Haiyan, lost a jade and diamond ring, a gold ring, a gold watch chain, a diamond platinum wristwatch, a jade bracelet, a gold cigarette holder, a gold toothpick, and over twenty yuan in cash. (2) Wang Jiahuan, from Tinglin, lost a gold watch. (3) Tao Taiqing, from Minhang, lost a gold ring and nineteen yuan in silver. (4) An accounting clerk from a Pinghu Huangxingji Flower Shop lost a check for 300 yuan and over ten yuan in cash, as well as over fifty yuan in cash from passengers surnamed Han and Wang, totaling approximately six thousand yuan.

Yesterday’s Thunderstorm Lasted Approximately Half an Hour 166

Temperature 95.7 Degrees

Since last week, the weather in this city has gradually turned cooler, with a refreshing autumn breeze. However, yesterday morning, it suddenly became hot and stuffy again. The Fahrenheit thermometer rose sharply to 95.7 degrees. Even when sitting quietly indoors, one was drenched in sweat. At 4:20 PM, the sky suddenly became covered with dark clouds, and a fierce northerly wind blew. In an instant, thunder and lightning roared, and a torrential downpour began. After about forty minutes, the rain began to subside, and it stopped completely at 5:40 PM. Many low-lying roads in both the Chinese and Foreign concessions of the city were flooded with two to three inches of water, which gradually receded after the rain stopped. The surrounding rural farmlands benefited greatly from this timely rain, with rice, cotton, and various vegetables all thriving. Farmers were universally delighted.

Chinese and Western Detectives Secretly Arrest 21 Gamblers 167

Arrested from Tongde Lane, Xihuaide Road

Since the authorities in charge of police affairs in both the Chinese and Foreign concessions of this city vigorously enforced the ban on gambling, many gamblers, unwilling to give up the lucrative business, moved to the Toyo Company dock in the American Concession of Hongkou. They rebuilt their operations, setting up tables in the open air or hiring large barges, moored in the Huangpu River, to gather gamblers to gamble on the boats. They also gambled in the cabins of ocean-going vessels docked at various wharves. Now, they are renting secret rooms in various alleys in Hongkou to gamble and collect commissions. They dispatched police to guard the front and back doors, then stormed in. At that time, there were seventy or eighty gamblers inside, gambling and shouting with great enthusiasm. They were arrested. However, due to the large number of gamblers, many escaped. In the end, 21 gamblers, including Wu Xingen (also known as Blind Xingen), Shen Alai (also known as Salted Meat Alai), Jiangbei Da Mao, Nanchang A Gen (also known as Little A Gen), Zhang Zhenhan, Zhang Ading, Wang Fuji, Shen Wanshan, Little Suzhou, and Chen Xiaohui, were arrested, along with gambling equipment, including shaking cylinders, silver boxes, chips, cash, and tables and benches. They were all taken to the police station to await investigation.

Counterfeit Money Den Broken Up in Panjiawan, Zhabei 169

Price of 100 Yuan is 8 Yuan

Five Criminals Arrested in Disguise

Liu Xueyou, a Yancheng native living in Tanjiazhai Panjiawan in Zhabei who worked as a rickshaw puller, Xiang Zhongyu, a Qinghe native who worked in the house at No. 100 Panjiawan, and Zhou Bingxiu, a barber who worked in a straw house opposite the old station on Zhongxing Road, etc., routinely bought five-yuan counterfeit banknotes of the China Industrial Bank and the Central Bank, etc., totaling 20 banknotes, equivalent to 100 yuan, at a price of 8 yuan, from secret counterfeit currency manufacturing organizations. They then went to various markets in the city to use them, making considerable profits. Liu and the others planned to continue buying and selling. However, their scheme was discovered by Dong Wenrui, deputy leader of the investigation team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Dong Wenrui reported the situation of Liu and the others using counterfeit banknotes to the leader of the investigation team, Lu Ying, who dispatched male and female detectives, along with the police officers of the fourth district, to disguise themselves and go to No. 100 Panjiawan on the evening of the day before yesterday, pretending to be vendors to trade with Liu. As a result, five counterfeit five-yuan banknotes of the China Industrial Bank, a Kunshan County Public Security Bureau detective's license, twenty-one pawn tickets, and seven bullets were found in Liu's house. One counterfeit five-yuan banknote of the Central Bank was also found on Xiang Zhongyu. In addition to arresting Liu Xueyou and Xiang Zhongyu, five accomplices, including Jiang Yunqing (also known as Jiang Wu), a Yancheng native, Zhou Bingxiu, a Qinghe native, and Tian Jiazong, an Anhui native, were also arrested. The counterfeit banknotes and evidence were taken to the investigation team for detention. Yesterday morning, Liu confessed under interrogation that Xiang Zhongyu had given him these twenty-five yuan of counterfeit banknotes of the China Industrial Bank. When the other criminals were questioned, they gave evasive answers. Team leader Lu believed that the case involved the use of counterfeit banknotes and the illegal possession of firearms, which not only disrupted the financial order but also violated the law. Therefore, he ordered that Liu Xueyou and the other five criminals, along with the counterfeit banknote evidence, be sent to the Third Section of the General Bureau yesterday afternoon to be dealt with according to the law.

Zhang Xiqi, Director of Guanghua Eye Hospital, Suddenly Disappears 171

Zhang Was Originally from Taiwan and Changed His Registration to Fujian

Missing for Three Days Without Any News

Was He Kidnapped or Abducted?

Zhang Xiqi, the director of Guanghua Eye Hospital at No. 116 Weier Meng Road in the French Concession, suddenly disappeared at 9:00 AM on the 1st of this month while going out for a consultation. For three days, there has been no news. Only yesterday did Zhang's family become alarmed and report the details to the police station, which are recorded below:

Originally from Taiwan 172

Zhang Xiqi, a Fujian native, is 37 years old, young, capable, and patriotic. Zhang was originally from a prominent family in Taiwan. Because he was saddened by the island of Taiwan falling into foreign hands and ashamed to be a subject of the foreigners, he changed his registration to Fujian. He studied in Japan in his early years and had the ambition to be a good doctor rather than a good official, specializing in ophthalmology. However, Zhang's words and actions at that time were already noticed by the Japanese authorities.

Coming to Shanghai 173

While studying in Japan, Zhang married a Japanese woman and had a daughter, who is now eight years old. After completing his studies, Zhang first took his wife back to Taiwan and founded the Zhonghua Association. Because he handled affairs fairly, he was admired by the overseas Chinese. Four years ago, he came to Shanghai and rented a house at No. 2 Hongan Lane, Luban Road in the French Concession. He first established the Guanghua Eye Hospital on Lao Bazi Road and also served as a professor of ophthalmology at Southeast Medical College. The relationship between teachers and students was excellent. When the January 28th Incident occurred, he moved to No. 116 Weier Meng Road in the French Concession last spring and continued to call it Guanghua Eye Hospital. Because Zhang's medical skills were profound, those seeking treatment always achieved success. As a result, his medical practice was very prosperous.

Deeply Patriotic 174

In order to expand his medical practice, Zhang also established a branch on No. 810 North Sichuan Road and hired Zheng Guoshun, a Cantonese, as his assistant (Zheng is 24 years old). Because Zhang specialized in ophthalmology, he invented a secret medicinal liquid, which was widely sold in the Shantou and Xiamen areas. Zhang's younger brother managed this business near Xiamen and often wrote to his younger brother, instructing him to use some of the profits to help the poor compatriots in Taiwan. This demonstrates Zhang's patriotism.

Invited to Make a House Call 175

At 7:30 AM on the 1st of this month, Zhang first went from his residence on Luban Road to Weier Meng Road for a consultation, which continued until 9:15 AM. Suddenly, an uninvited guest wearing a coffee-colored long silk robe and speaking in the local dialect came to the registration desk and asked Zhang to make a house call. After paying the fee, the guest turned and left. At that time, Zhang did not pay any attention. Around 11:00 AM, when Zhang's consultations were just about to end, the guest hurriedly returned and called three rickshaws, urging Zhang to leave.

Gone and Never Returned 176

Zhang asked where they were going, and the guest replied, "Nanyang Bridge." Zhang then instructed his assistant, Zheng Guoshun, to bring the medicine kit and follow the guest out the door, taking a rickshaw south. Who would have known that he would never return? Zhang's family waited until that evening but still did not see him come home. They knew something was wrong but did not dare to make it public immediately. At the same time, they sent out scouts, but for three days, there has been no trace of him, and there are no clues.

Someone Asked for a Loan 177

Until yesterday, the family was at their wits' end and had no choice but to report the matter to the police station and ask for assistance. The police chief immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. According to Zhang's family, in the ten days before the incident, someone had sent two letters using the envelopes and stationery of the Oriental Hotel, asking Zhang for a loan. The letters were signed with the surname "Xiao," but Zhang, having no connection with the sender, declined, saying that he was not at home. The original letters were immediately returned. According to general speculation, the case is bizarre and may be a kidnapping. Some people said that Zhang's disappearance may be the same as the previous kidnapping of the Korean Li Chunshan. We will record it to see what happens later. According to Zhang's nephew, who spoke to our reporter, Zhang usually stayed at home and had very few friends. Moreover, his family was poor and had no savings. When Zhang's wife returned to Japan for medical treatment, she borrowed 200 yuan from a friend for expenses. His sudden disappearance is really beyond our expectations.

Creditors of Riyue Bank File a Lawsuit Against Partner Shareholders 178

Should Bear Joint and Several Liability

The various details of the Gongfa Company, affiliated with the Shanghai Riyue Bank, declaring bankruptcy and liquidation since the death of its founder, Huang Chu Jiu, have been repeatedly reported in the previous newspapers. Now, creditors Xu Peiyuan, Heji, Wang Qitao, Pan Binji, Zhang Lieji, Liu Qishen, Cheng Kefan, Xie Shuji, etc., have recently hired lawyers Bian Jialu, Dong Yu, and Zhou Xiaoan to file a lawsuit with the Mediation Office of the Civil Court of the Second Special District Court. The main points of their application are: requesting confirmation of partnership, clarifying responsibilities, and facilitating liquidation matters. The applicants had previously deposited money into the Shanghai Riyue Bank. In addition to compensating for the liquidation of the company's assets, the remaining amount should be borne by the shareholders. However, since the liquidation of the case has exceeded three years, each creditor has only been allocated 20% of their claim, and the remaining executable assets are very small, making it difficult to compensate for the losses. The Gongfa Company was originally a partnership, which has been confirmed by the Supreme Court. When the partnership assets are insufficient to repay the partnership's debts, each partner is jointly and severally liable for the shortfall, as clearly stipulated in Article 681 of the Civil Code. Wang Yutai Tea Company, Huayang Pharmacy, Liu Jiaji, etc. are all partner shareholders of the Gongfa Company. Therefore, they request mediation to confirm that the respondents are partners of the Gongfa Company and should bear joint and several liability for the Gongfa Company's debts. The court has approved the request and held a hearing for mediation, which was adjourned. Yesterday morning, they were summoned again, and Judge Li Liang continued the mediation in Civil Court Seven. Wang Yutai was represented by lawyer Zhang Yaozeng, who denied joining the Gongfa Company as a shareholder. Huayang Pharmacy was represented by lawyers Li Guozhen and Lu Shifang, who stated that their client had purchased 300 yuan in stocks. However, the company was not legally registered and therefore has no legal effect under civil law. Since there is no legal registration, their client is not responsible. Liu Jiaji was represented by lawyer Wu Zhiping, who stated that their client had never bought shares in the Gongfa Company. Judge Li ordered them to leave and await another hearing.

Magic Scam Where One Banknote Becomes Two, Huge Amount of Money 179

Shen Baohe Lost 5,000 Yuan

French Police Formally File Lawsuit

Shen Baohe, a Wuxi native, 33 years old, runs the Dexing Printing House at No. 7 Wenxian Lane, Lafayette Road in the French Concession. On April 8th of this year, Ji Pingshan, an acquaintance, told Shen that the Westerner Bai Lishi's foreign firm at No. 3 Huanlong Road needed a lot of account books and was willing to introduce him. At that time, for business purposes, Shen followed Ji. When they arrived at their destination, they waited in the reception room. After a while, a Chinese man, Pei Zhongying, came out to meet them. Ji introduced him to Shen. Pei claimed that he and the Westerner Bai Lishi could use magic to turn one yuan banknote into two one-yuan banknotes. If you used 1,000 yuan or 10,000 yuan banknotes, they could turn them into 2,000 or 20,000 respectively. But it had to be cash. Shen was fooled and driven by greed. He agreed to raise money immediately, so he went home and tried to borrow money from his brother Shen Baochang and friends.

Page 16

He managed to borrow 1,900 yuan in China Industrial Bank banknotes, 1,000 yuan in British gold pounds, and 3,200 yuan in various other bank notes, totaling 5,000 yuan. On the evening of April 25th, he went with Ji Pingshan to a Western-style house at No. 74 Huanlong Road, where Pei Zhongying and the Westerner Bai Lishi were waiting. Shen gave the money to them. They led Shen to a dark room, under the pretext of performing magic, and there was a loud bang, like a movie sound. After a while, the Westerner excused himself and left, and all the money had been taken away. At that time, Shen questioned Ji and Pei, and Ji and the others issued a letter of responsibility, stating that they would return the money the next day. Unexpectedly, they disappeared. Until the day before yesterday, Shen ran into Pei Zhongying on Yan Hai Street in the Chinese Concession and immediately called the police to arrest him. Under interrogation, because the incident occurred in the French Concession, the two parties were transferred to the French Police. Yesterday, they were sent to the Second Special District Court, and the police lawyer charged them with fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Law. Because the case was not yet clear, they requested an extension to investigate before another hearing. After a brief interrogation by the judge, he ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and adjourned the hearing to investigate further.

The Red Pill Factory on Ningguo Road Was Founded by a Japanese National 180

Japanese National Fukuda Hiding Without a Trace

Chinese Associates Awaiting Sentencing

Detectives Li Pengfei and Wu Shoushan of the Yulin Road Police Station, along with Western detectives, raided a red pill manufacturing factory at the Nishima Winery on Ningguo Road at 11:45 AM on the 27th of last month. They arrested five people, including Yao Fuyuan, Chen Bobiao, and Zheng Jinfa from Fujian, Li Zike from Anhui, and Wang Shixing from Changshu, and sent them, along with various machines and a large amount of medicinal powder, heroin, and morphine, to the First Special District Court. It was revealed that the factory was founded by a Japanese national named Fukuda, who is currently at large. The hearing was postponed to re-examine various aspects. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui presided over a continuation of the hearing in Criminal Court Three. Industrial Board lawyer Li Zhishan stated that during the postponement, a notebook containing entry and exit figures was found in the home of the first defendant, Yao Fuyuan, in the French Concession. A ledger showing the start of construction of the factory was found in the small room where Chen Bobiao, accused of being at No. 117 Ningguo Road, lived. Yao, Chen, and Zheng claimed to have been associates with the Japanese national Fukuda. Li and Wang were hired personnel. There were many instruments in the factory. Photos have been taken and detailed accounts have been made. There were also three large bags of medicinal powder, which were tested by Industrial Board doctors and found to contain heroin and morphine. The ledgers, photos, and medicinal powder were presented. Fukuda, the Japanese national, is hiding and is now being prosecuted under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. When questioned, the defendants' confessions were similar to their previous statements. Yao Fuyuan was represented by lawyer Jiang Yiping. Judge Liu ordered them to be remanded in custody for sentencing at a later date.

Another Criminal Investigated in the Excavation of the Ji Juemi Family Ancestral Tomb 181

The Gatekeeper of Cihou Lane

Arrested Inside Hardoon & Co.

Ji Juemi, the General Manager of Hardoon & Co. on Nanjing Road, and a native of Xuzhou, had his family ancestral tomb in Panjiazhuang excavated by local bandits between November of last year and March of this year. The remains were stolen and hidden, and a letter was sent to the Ji family demanding a large ransom. Zhang Huaiqing, a Xuzhou native and leader of the bandits in the case, was arrested by the Yangshupu Police Station and sentenced to seven years in prison by the First Special District Court, where he is currently serving his sentence. Zhang's arrest was due to Qiu Yongzhi, the gatekeeper of No. 38 Cihou Lane on Hardoon Road, who had tricked him into coming to Shanghai from Wuxi. Because Suining County in Xuzhou found that Qiu was also involved in the damage to the tombs in Panjiazhuang, the General Patrol Office received an official letter from the county requesting his arrest. A warrant was issued to Detective Liu Xiangzhai of the First Special Court, who secretly went to Hardoon & Co. on Nanjing Road to arrest Qiu. Yesterday morning, he was sent to Criminal Court One. Police lawyer Gan Jingxian stated the previous events, and when the defendant denied them, Chief Judge Qian Hongye ordered him to be remanded in custody, and Suining County was given two weeks to provide sufficient evidence for review.

Child Burned to Death 182

Fear of Repeated Childbirth Failure

Parents Took Drastic Measures

At around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, Officer No. 1896 of the Putuo Road Police Station, while patrolling in Nanyinghua Lane on Laobasheng Road, discovered the body of a dead infant, estimated to be only three or four months old. The child's body was burned all over. The police station was notified and ordered detectives to investigate, and the child's body was taken to the Feilun Road mortuary. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Tang was dispatched by the First Special Court to inspect and confirm the body. It was found that the deceased was a nameless infant whose body had been burned after dying of illness. There were no relatives. The body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial. Judging from the above, it must have been the parents who repeatedly failed to have children and took this superstitious measure to pray that their future children would be able to be cared for. Such cases have been seen many times in Shanghai.

Another New Large Wharf Completed in Shanghai 183

Located in Lujiazui

Named Taitong Wharf

In recent years, the number of ships entering and leaving the port of Shanghai has increased day by day, and the demand for wharves and warehouses has exceeded the supply. Foreign freighters often have no place to dock. Chinese businessman Wang Zhongzhi and others have invested heavily in building a large wharf in Lujiazui, with warehouses attached. The wharf is seven or eight hundred feet long and can simultaneously dock one ocean-going vessel and one coastal vessel. The three warehouses have a huge storage capacity and are twenty-five feet deep at low tide, so even presidential liners and queen ships can dock without any problem. The project is nearing completion and is named Taitong. In addition, a railway track will be built on the wharf, directly connecting to the warehouses. Ships loading and unloading cargo can use machines to transport them to the warehouses (or from the warehouses to the ships), which will not only reduce huge handling costs but also speed up the process. The customs inspection room and office space in the warehouse have been completed one after another and are scheduled to start operations this month. It is also reported that the wharf will be managed by the American firm Shihua & Co.

National Medicine Industry Entertains Reporters 184

Opposing Ningbo Xiangbei Transportation and Sales Cooperative Speculating and Hoarding

The Shanghai National Medicine Industry Association hosted over twenty members of the Shanghai press last night. Committee member Cen Zhiliang reported, saying, "Esteemed gentlemen, our association has prepared a simple feast today, and we are deeply honored by your presence. The significance of inviting you here today is twofold. Firstly, since our association was established last August, we have had few opportunities to interact with you. Therefore, we would like to seek your guidance to improve our shortcomings. Secondly, we would like to take this opportunity to inform you about the actual situation of the Xiangbei incident, which is about to erupt, and ask you to provide fair criticism. Xiangbei is a specialty product of Zhangcun, Ningbo. Its uses have gradually expanded over the years, and its historical selling price has been approximately 40 to 80 yuan. Since the establishment of the Yin County Dongjiang Fritillaria Transportation and Sales Cooperative last year, the products have been concentrated in the cooperative, which has colluded with Baohe, Baosheng, Huiyuan, Maocheng, and other four medicine stores, monopolizing and speculating, hoarding goods to raise prices, and doing whatever they want. In three or four months, the price has soared to over 150 yuan. However, in reality, the farmers are still puppets, and there are also production restrictions planned to create a supply shortage. Our association firmly opposed this in the first meeting of member representatives last August. The cooperative and the four medicine stores sent representatives to Shanghai to invite Mr. Zhang Shenzhi and Mr. Fang Jiaobo, fellow Ningbo natives, to mediate. An agreement was signed at that time, in which the second clause stated that 'any increase or decrease in production and agreement on prices must be discussed and implemented with the participation of our association representatives,' which is the spirit of the entire agreement. However, the cooperative and the four medicine stores actually used primitive methods to restrict production, causing panic in the market. At the same time, the price suddenly rose to over 300 yuan, increasing the burden on patients and disregarding the contract. The national medical community in this city unanimously believes that this behavior needs to be corrected. Our association has now decided not to purchase Xiangbei, and various national medical organizations have also notified their members to use Qianhu as a substitute. Our association hopes to restore the original situation after achieving a considerable result, otherwise, we will persist to the end and never abandon our position."

National Medical Organizations Discuss the Monopoly of Xiangbei 185

Xiangbei is one of the national medicines, produced in Yin County, Zhejiang Province. The price per dan has traditionally been 30 to 40 yuan, up to 60 to 70 yuan. Since the establishment of the Yinjiang Fritillaria Transportation and Sales Cooperative, Xiangbei has been centrally transported and sold, prohibiting farmers from selling freely. This year, production was further restricted, prohibiting the digging of Xiangbei that should have been unearthed in April, resulting in an increase in the price per dan to over 300 yuan. The Shanghai national medicine industry believes that this kind of monopolistic means directly increases the cost of the industry and indirectly increases the burden on patients. If various medicinal material producing areas follow suit, the consequences would be unimaginable. Therefore, they requested assistance from national medical organizations. The Shanghai Municipal National Medical Association, Shanghai National Medical Society, Shenzhou National Medical Society, and中华 National Medical Society jointly sent a letter to the cooperative to inquire, but have not yet received a reply. Therefore, representatives were elected last night to meet at the National Medical Association to decide on sanctions, hoping to act in unison with the national medicine industry.

Tobacco Exchange Industry Again Requests Reduction of License Tax 186

Before the Re-examination is Completed

Requesting Exemption from Fines

Since the Shanghai tobacco and alcohol license tax has been taken over by the Finance Bureau, the two types of ding tobacco and bing alcohol must be rectified according to regulations and changed to bing and yi levels. Various small tobacco exchange shops believe that the doubled tax is too heavy and claim that they cannot afford it. They have asked the association to earnestly request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to ask the Finance Bureau to verify and reduce the collection. The association petitioned the Chamber of Commerce on the 29th of last month and discussed relief measures. The previous list of names was sent to the Finance Bureau for review and reduction. Those who have not yet reported should be notified again to submit a supplementary report within one week, stating the reasons for being unable to afford the tax, so that the request can be forwarded. According to the Shanghai South Office of the association, after issuing a notice on its own, those who reported for registration in the past few days were very crowded and did not stop until 6 pm. The deadline is today, and the list will be completed and reported tomorrow. It is also reported that investigators from the Tax Collection Office are urging various shops to pay the increased tax and threatening to issue licenses within three days, otherwise, they will be fined. After the association received the report, it publicly appointed Chen Liangyu and Zhang Songji to visit the Municipal Chamber of Commerce again tomorrow to ask Chairman Yu to earnestly request the authorities to exempt them from fines before the re-examination of the added tax amount is completed.

Palette Trademark Appeal Rejected 192

Jiufu Company Still Maintains Victory in Trademark Law

Jiufu Company's various Tonic Pills are very effective in treating the lungs and strengthening the body, surpassing all other medicines. The American company Pade has constantly been involved in disputes with it over the Palette trademark. Until the beginning of the year, the position of Tonic Pills in trademark law, through the interpretation of the Judicial Yuan and the decision of the Ministry of Industry, Jiufu Company finally won the final victory. Unexpectedly, Pade Company still appealed to the Executive Yuan recently, but because its reasons were weak and insufficient to shake the final ruling, it was rejected. Jiufu Company still maintains the victory in the Tonic Pills trademark. It is also heard that Jiufu Company's Tonic Pills, in addition to the original pure and containing Jiguai types, has also added three types containing iodine, arsenic, and quinine, making a total of five types. Among them, the pure type is necessary for those with weak bodies, the type containing Jiguai treats coughs and pulmonary tuberculosis, the type containing iodine is suitable for various chronic diseases, the type containing arsenic is suitable for blood deficiency and neurasthenia, and the type containing quinine is suitable for those with a bad taste. Each has miraculous effects, so sales are very large.

A Hooligan Opens Fire and Injures Someone Over a Disagreement 193

Liu Jinfa, a 21-year-old from Hangzhou, lives at No. 22 Rusheng Lane, Wuhua Road, under the jurisdiction of the Third Precinct of the Fifth District of Zhabei. He has been working as a laborer in a nearby silk weaving factory. At about 9:30 pm last night, Liu felt stuffy in the house and was cooling off at the door. At that time, his neighbor, a hooligan named Shen Laosan, was also outside enjoying the cool and chatting with two or three of his kind. Unexpectedly, they started fighting over a disagreement. However, Shen Laosan was no match for the crowd, so in desperation, he pulled out the gun he was carrying and fired at the other hooligans. Unexpectedly, those hooligans saw the opportunity and dodged. Liu Jinfa was behind them and could not escape in time. The bullet hit Liu's abdomen, and he fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Shen Laosan and others saw that they had caused trouble and fled one after another. By the time the nearby police officer arrived, they had already escaped far away. They rushed Liu Jinfa to Baolong Hospital for treatment and reported back to the precinct to pursue the escaped hooligan Shen Laosan and others for investigation.

Two Cars Collide, and a Datong Student is Injured 194

Zhou Rongxin, 21 years old, and Zhou Jianxiang, 19 years old, both students from Datong University and natives of Guangdong, hired a Yunfei Automobile Company car with teachers and classmates from the school to come to Shanghai at about 8 pm last night. Unexpectedly, when the car drove near No. 320 Yuyuan Road, Shanghai West, the driver of the car carelessly collided with a No. 1 public bus coming from the opposite direction. Inventors of Chinese Typing and Shorthand Co-operate to Run a Special School 195

Chinese typing and Chinese shorthand are two major inventions of modern times. Not only do various institutions in the country hire personnel in these fields to save money and time, but also factories and foreign firms established by foreigners have purchased machines one after another and entrusted Yu Binqi, the inventor of the Chinese typewriter, and Yang Bingxun, the inventor of Chinese shorthand, to find specialized talents. Mr. Yu and Mr. Yang, in view of this, in addition to cooperating with various famous schools in Shanghai, have recently jointly established a Chinese Typing and Shorthand School in Shanchang Lane, Kad Road, to teach the knowledge of both subjects and create experts proficient in both. Fearing that students' foundations in Chinese studies are weak, unfamiliar with official document formats, and unable to obtain superior positions, they have specially hired Mr. Hu Tiewu as the dean of the school. Mr. Hu has held important positions in both political and academic circles, and his students number in the thousands. This time, as he presides over academic affairs, he will definitely develop more. Moreover, in order to achieve the purpose of applying what they have learned, the school guarantees employment for all graduates. It is heard that the school only accepts 20 students, and the quota is almost full. Classes are scheduled to start on the 17th of this month.

Weather Report 200

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that Shandong is cloudy all around, with showers and strong northeasterly winds. There are cyclones and rain in the Yellow Sea, caused by the passage of a low-pressure system moving eastward. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and this area are cloudy, with thunderstorms and variable winds. The East China Sea is cloudy, with strong northeasterly winds. The weather around Taiwan is very bad, due to the passage of a hurricane east of Luzon moving northwestward. The second hurricane has landed on the coast of Annam and is moving northwest-westward. The center of the hurricane was at 2 pm yesterday within 60 miles of the intersection of 18 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude, moving northwestward, with violent winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 2 pm yesterday, the temperature in this city was a maximum of 95.7 and a minimum of 73.0. On the same day last year, the maximum was 89.1 and the minimum was 72.3.

Letter 202

To the Editor: I was extremely surprised to read a news item in your esteemed newspaper of the 4th of this month stating that the Mainland Bazaar would be adding an amusement park. Upon investigation, the design of our bazaar is that the storefronts are along the road, the second floor is the bazaar, and the third floor and above are all office spaces. Major commercial establishments in Shanghai, appreciating the grand architecture and superior location, are vying to rent, and the office spaces are particularly in short supply. Recently, we have added dozens of new-style office spaces on the seventh floor, which have been completed and are now being rented. There is no plan to add an amusement park. Fearing that rumors outside are untrue, we hereby issue a special letter of correction to clarify the facts. Sincerely, Mainland Bazaar Office. 23.9.4.

Reading News

25th Issue

Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shenbao Circulation Library

Continued Table of Contents 203

(1) This Doesn't Count··········

(2) Book Introductions······ (Continued)

(3) This Week's Broadcast

2. Introducing the September Issue of "Middle School Student"

"Middle School Student" magazine, anyone who is even slightly concerned about regular periodicals probably already knows it, right? It has a five-year history, and has not only become the only extracurricular reading for middle school students, but also a good companion for general shop assistants, apprentices, and other amateurs. As long as you have a high school education, you can understand it.

The articles in this September issue are worth our special attention; such as Jin Zhonghua's "From Learning to Application" which starts from the current situation where the Tianjin University graduates are forming an employment alliance asking for help from all parties, and discusses the social origin of the contradictory phenomenon of the outflow of current school graduates, or learning that is not used, and "using what is not learned". It is extremely insightful and thorough. Mao Dun's "The Iliad and the Odyssey" is the first article in the series of lectures on famous literary works that began in this issue. Have readers who love literature heard of these two of the world's oldest literary masterpieces? But China does not yet have a translated version (the Odyssey has recently been published by the Commercial Press), and even when mentioned, it is very brief. Here, using extremely popular means, the author discusses the era of the original work, the artistic skill of the author, the content of the story, and similar works in literary history (this is according to the editor's postscript, because this issue has not been completely published). If this lecture starts from ancient times until recently, it will become a very popular history of literature. Zhang Mingyang's International Politics Lectures started in the January issue of this year. Each issue is an article, and each article is independent. It is good to read them together, but it is also okay to separate them. This issue is an article on the issue of war debts. This issue has been a very serious issue on the international stage in the past ten years, and you can almost see it every time you open the newspaper. But what exactly is the content of this issue? Why is it so serious and delayed for more than ten years without a solution? Or maybe many readers are wondering? Then this article is the answer to these questions. I know that there are many readers who are studying social sciences. Most of what is said in ordinary books are general principles and past events. If you want to connect what you have learned with everything in reality and get a thorough understanding, then you must read this type of article and the news in the newspaper.

Regarding natural sciences, this issue has Gu Junzheng's "Talk about Tides" and Xu Chunfang's "Old Studies Lectures", both of which are narrated in a storytelling tone, which is very interesting to read, and completely different from the boring and dullness of general textbooks. The remaining essays, occasional talks, cultural news, etc. are all like this, and we can call them "scientific essays." The final English column is also newly added this year, which is very helpful for those who are studying English on their own.

In short, the aspects included in this are very broad. Although the length is not very long, they are all very exciting. Although readers have different interests, they can all obtain the spiritual food they need.

3. This Week's Broadcast

If readers have any questions about wireless radio science and medicine in the future, please send them directly to the editorial department of this newspaper's Wireless Radio Weekly and Medicine Weekly, and we will reply in detail.

Special Item

Reducing Road Transportation Prices and Developing the Rural Economy Wu Shaozeng 204

Railways hold the hub of a country's transportation. In addition to solving some transportation and national defense issues, they are responsible for promoting social and economic policies. For example, railways in the East and West have very low ratings for industrial raw materials and people's daily necessities, and charge extremely low freight rates to help promote the prosperity of the national economy. Judging from the current national situation in our country, the bankruptcy of the rural economy has plunged all industrial and commercial enterprises into a state of decline and ruin, which is a injury to the entire national and national life. If we want to enrich national strength and turn the national fortune around, we must concentrate the thoughts, minds and talents of the entire country to restore the rural economy. This principle has long been recognized by the people of the country. Even the government is also using this as a starting point in its planning and thinking. Therefore, how to solve the rural economic problem, at the present stage, is the center of the entire social and economic policy, and the railway must assist in the implementation of this policy, in order to not fail its mission. Whether it is state-owned or private, it is its due obligation, and there is no room for hesitation or observation. (To be continued)

The Second Batch of Summer Military Training in This City Will Soon Be Completed 211

Director Jiao Has Been Personally Inspecting the Various Schools in Recent Days

He Spoke Freely Yesterday About Various Issues Regarding Military Training in Schools in This City

The second batch of summer military training for high schools and above in this city is about to be completed. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency visited Jiao Jihua, the director of the National Military Training Committee, and spoke freely about various issues regarding the implementation of national military education in this city for over an hour. The key points are recorded below.

The Second Batch of Military Training Will Soon Be Completed 212

The reporter first inquired about the situation of the second batch of military training in this city. According to him, the second batch of summer military training in schools in this city, which started around the 20th of last month, will be completed within this week, after two weeks. He had visited various schools in recent days to inspect the results, which were generally satisfactory. However, due to the impact of various issues such as school funding and the allocation of instructors, shortcomings were inevitable. However, the spirit is especially important. To achieve good results in military training, the first year must inspire the students' spirit, make them understand that to preserve Chinese culture, it is necessary to first develop the national defense forces, and that young students should stand at the forefront to lead the general public. If they can understand this principle and receive military training, the effect will be significant. In addition to the government's strict implementation, it also depends on the school authorities' promotion and the society's encouragement to promote students' awareness, so as to achieve the purpose of implementing military training.

Full Implementation Starting This Semester 213

Jiao also said that national military training includes a wide range of aspects and is not limited to military training in schools. Military training for merchants and workers should also be implemented. However, due to the lack of a fixed group and a strict organization among the industrial and commercial sectors, as well as various factors such as funding, it will be difficult to realize in the short term. Therefore, the central government will first start with schools in the first year of national military education in various places. Currently, there are only over thirty schools in this city that have military training, including universities and high schools. There are more high schools and above in the city than this number. Therefore, the schools that have not received military training will implement it across the board starting this semester. The military instructors for each school will be dispatched by the General Training Headquarters in the coming days to serve.

Schools Are Not Allowed to Use Instructors Privately 214

Regarding students in schools who fail military training, they should comply with the ministry's order and strictly enforce it, and not allow them to be promoted. Secondly, military instructors should not be hired privately. Military instructors cannot be treated the same as science teachers. The science taught by science teachers is the same principle in all countries, but military science differs from country to country. For example, the organization and tactics have special training. Therefore, the central government requires that military instructors for each school must be submitted to the Military Affairs Committee for approval, and graduates of the instructor training class should be sent to fill the positions, and each school must not appoint them without authorization, in order to achieve uniformity.

Change the Training Method Next Year 215

Finally, when the reporter asked whether the summer military training next year would still be conducted in the same way as this year, it was said that the Ministry of Education and the General Training Headquarters had consulted on the matter and decided that, starting next year, all first-year high school and first-year university students must receive three months of centralized training from April to July. The intention is to have the high school and university students complete their military training at once after enrollment, instead of the staggered approach of the past. This training cultivates ordinary soldiers in high school and military officers in universities. Currently, this city lacks barracks for centralized training, and preparations are actively underway for the implementation of centralized military training next year.

Special Reports

The Problem of Civic Education in National Revival (3) by Zhang Yuanruo 221

Unfortunately, later scholars not only failed to understand Confucius' profound and extensive principles of civic education, but also outwardly complied and inwardly disobeyed, completely burying Confucius' legacy, leading to the daily decline of public morale and the weakening of national power. If the doctrines and principles of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, the Duke of Zhou, and Confucius could be promoted and developed generation after generation, I believe that China today would not only not be so weak, but would have become the strongest country in the world. If you think my words are too grand and baseless, just look at Japan to be convinced. There are many reasons why Japan is so strong, but one important reason is that they were able to inherit our inherent culture and develop it, which created the foundation for Japan's strength (see Dai Jitao, "On Japan"). However, we Chinese ourselves could not inherit our own inherent culture and develop it to strengthen ourselves, but instead allowed others to inherit it and strengthen their country, which is extremely regrettable. In form, our country has always respected Confucius, but in reality, it is not Confucius who dominates the thinking of the Chinese people, but Lao Tzu (the reasons for this need to be explained in another article, which cannot be detailed here). Lao Tzu's thought is a philosophy of extreme individualism. Because this philosophy is extremely individualistic, it is extremely selfish and extremely passive. Because of the result of this extremely selfish and extremely passive individualistic education, it denies human relationships, denies the organization of the state, and destroys social morality. Therefore, although the Chinese nation has a history of more than 4,000 years, it is still scolded as an unorganized country. The reason why our country is unorganized is because it has been poisoned by this extremely selfish and extremely passive individualism, so that the general public not only do not know the responsibilities they should bear to the state and society, but also completely destroy our country's inherent education for organizing the state and managing society.

By the time of the Wei, Jin, and Southern and Northern Dynasties, this extremely selfish and passive individualism became even more corrupt and intensified. The people at that time only sought personal comfort, ease, and enjoyment, and the decadent and romantic nature of individualism became even more intensified. Because of the development of the decadent and romantic nature of individualism, the social activity of our people disappeared, and the sense of social responsibility also disappeared. At the same time, the people's desire for upward mobility also completely disappeared. At that time, the people showed no spirit of responsibility and upward mobility. Therefore, the Chinese people's inherent spirit of creating culture and cherishing the country and society was completely suppressed by this decadent and romantic nature of individualism, and it became a powerful evil force in history that dominated our national life. This evil force has since dominated China for thousands of years.

By the late Qing Dynasty, when foreign forces invaded and the national power declined, there was a so-called Reform Movement. The characteristics of the Reform Movement are two. First, the so-called "Chinese learning for the foundation, Western learning for application." The so-called Western learning for application is to strengthen armor, sharpen weapons, and expand military preparations. However, the activity of our people has been almost completely lost. Even with sharp guns, it is impossible to use them. Second, Kang Youwei's reform. He thought that if the country was to be strong, it would only be necessary to change the law. Kang's theory also failed to address the root cause. Because the evil force that has dominated our national character for thousands of years, in other words, is the decadent and romantic nature of individualism that is not upward, not responsible, and not striving. If it is not eradicated from the root, reform is in vain. The result will inevitably fail. Therefore, the Reform Movement still failed to revive China in the end. Japan's Reform Movement was at the same time as ours, but they succeeded. The reason for their success is that they were able to focus on the essentials and cultivate their national strength. However, our Reform Movement failed to start from the root and failed to fundamentally transform the inferior nature of our people, so that they could move upward and strive forward. Naturally, there was no possibility of success. Later, Mr. Liang Qichao founded the "New Citizen Journal" and advocated the theory of the New Citizen. He wanted to fundamentally reform the nation and revitalize the people's hearts. He can be said to be my comrade. His remarks published in the "New Citizen Journal" at that time, such as advocating public morality, martial spirit, patriotism, altruism, adventure, and introducing Western academics, were all very important. However, although Mr. Liang Qichao's articles were very sharp and his spirit was very magnificent, did they really touch the hearts of the people of the whole country? I think most of you present have read Mr. Liang Qichao's articles. When you read his articles, you must have been moved by him. However, our many sentient beings in the whole country were still indifferent and unmoved. This is because his advocacy did not penetrate the people universally, so he still failed to save our nation. This is what I especially want to hope that all of you teachers present will pay close attention to and continue to work hard on.

Since then, the people of the country, in view of the failure of the imperial examination system, have also advocated new learning. However, after advocating new learning, a new morbidity has occurred, which is the Europeanization that does not conform to national conditions. Because this kind of Europeanized education does not meet the needs of our nation, does not understand the history, national conditions, and characteristics of our inherent culture, the result is that the general public in China do not even know the names of various places in their own country, but know the place names of various Western countries. Even the textbooks on civics, history, and geography in their own country are adopted from foreign versions without selection. The most absurd thing is that the teachers of general universities, and even some middle schools, blindly use foreign languages in their lectures, questions, and school announcements. Therefore, what is trained by this kind of extreme Europeanized education is not Chinese citizens, but docile people who believe in the West. Can this new education revive the nation? Can it inspire the people's strong feelings for the country and the nation? Thinking of this, we cannot help but feel very sad. The May Fourth New Culture Movement originally bore a very important mission of the times. If it could be guided properly and carried out in a down-to-earth manner, it might not be an opportunity for the revival of our nation. However, unfortunately, a ghost followed this movement, which is romantic and uninhibited liberalism. Therefore, the Chinese nation still did not break away from the domination of the decadent and romantic nature of traditional individualism. Therefore, the May Fourth New Culture Movement did not produce any effect in the end. Until now, the situation in all aspects of the country and society has become increasingly deteriorated. You are all primary school teachers. What do you think of the current education compared to the past? How are the academic styles of the past and the present, the advantages and disadvantages? Social discipline, etc., are also getting worse and worse. The reason for this is probably the result of the trouble caused by liberalism, individualism, and romanticism. However, most people in society are still vaguely dominated by this extreme romanticism and are not aware of it. How can such a nation cheer up and generate strength?

I have now roughly reviewed this complex history from Yao, Shun, Tang, Wen, Wu, the Duke of Zhou to the New Culture Movement. From this historical process, we can see through the reasons for the decline of our nation. The historical reasons for the decline of this nation, briefly speaking, on the one hand, are that the principles of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, the Duke of Zhou, and Confucius, those who organized the state, organized society, and educated the people, have not been promoted and developed, while on the other hand, Lao Tzu's extremely self-interested individualism has dominated the hearts of the people for thousands of years, so that our people cannot have a relationship with society and the country, nor can they fulfill their responsibilities and exert their strength. Therefore, we only see the development of the decadent and romantic nature of individualism and selfishness, but do not see the people's sense of responsibility, upward mobility, and activity towards society and the country. This is the reason why the Chinese people cannot generate strength, and it is also the historical reason for the decline of our Chinese nation (see my book "The Road to Chinese Social Movement," published in the first issue of "Chinese Society" and Volume 5, Issue 1 of "Prospects").

3. The Reasons for the Development of Various Nationalities and the Observation of Their Citizenship. The Reasons for the Decline of the Chinese Nation Have Been Described Above. However, Why Can the Nationalities of Various Countries in the World Be Strong? The Reasons for This Are Worth Studying. Let's First Look at the Situation of the Western Nationalities. Whether They Are Large or Small, Western Nationalities Are Generally Very Strong. Even a Small Country Like Belgium Can Resist Germany, and Its Performance in Construction Is Admired by Various Countries. We Examine the Reasons for the Development of Their Nationalities. There Are Three.

1. The Development of Nationalism. Since the 19th century, nationalism in various Western countries has been greatly developed. Scholars in their countries have spared no effort in promoting nationalism. The most famous ones are Massii of Italy, Fichte, Hegel, Sauigng, Eluing, Eluntochli, Palman of Germany, and Raman and Larmati of France. Scholars and writers have all worked hard to promote nationalism in literature, political commentary, and law, and to arouse the national consciousness of the people. However, scholars and writers in our country mostly do not ask about politics, do not know the country, or indulge in poetry and wine, or play with things and lose their ambitions, or create new ideas and confuse the masses. Most of them lack strong national emotions. Therefore, in the past 100 years, there have been strong national movements in various European countries from the Baltic Sea to the Mediterranean Sea. These are all the achievements of their scholars and writers in working hard to promote the development of nationalism. Among them, the unification of Germany and Italy is the most important and spectacular historical event. However, we are still divided and fighting civil wars. Each of us is showing our selfish wisdom and disregarding the overall situation.

2. The Development of Social Morality. The Development of Social Morality Is Very Trivial to Talk About. I Can Only Briefly Talk About It Now. The So-Called Social Morality Is Actually Confucius' "Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness." Unfortunately, It Has Not Developed in China, But Has Run to the West to Develop. Various Western Countries Do Not Have Confucius, But They Have Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness. Although We Chinese Have Confucius, We Do Not Have Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness. This Is Why the Republic of China Is Declining, Chinese Society Is Chaotic, Western Nationalities Are Rising, and Western Society Is Well-Governed. I Remember When I Returned to China from Europe in the Past, I Was Invited to Give a Lecture for the First Time. The Chairman Asked Me to Tell Them About the Prosperous Situation in Foreign Countries. I Felt Very Pained at That Time and Said at the Beginning That You Will Definitely Be Disappointed After Listening to What I Am Going to Say Today. I Am Unwilling to Tell Everyone About the Prosperous Situation of Foreign Countries, Because the Material Civilization of Foreign Countries and the Extravagant Situation of Foreign Countries Have All Invaded Our Central Land. Just Go to Shanghai, Tianjin, and Guangzhou to See. You Can Understand It, So You Don't Need to Talk About It Anymore. What I Am Going to Talk About Today Is What We Chinese Ourselves Have Been Lost to Other Countries. There Is a Best Thing in Our Chinese History, Which Is Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness, Which Is Confucius' Legacy. However, We Chinese Cannot Find Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness Now. China Is Now Unkind, Unrighteous, Imprudent, and Untrustworthy, While Foreign Countries Have This Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness. Since I Met This National Treasure Lost to Other Countries in Foreign Countries, I Cannot Help But Report to You. I Feel That the Reason Why Western Society Has Developed Is Because of the Development of Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, and Trustworthiness. "Benevolence" Is a Kind of Social Sympathy. This Spirit of Westerners Is the Most Developed. It Can Be Seen Everywhere. Unlike Us Chinese Who See Someone Fall on the Road, We Not Only Do Not Help Him Up, But Also Clap Our Hands and Laugh. Speaking of "Righteousness," Chinese People Are Lazy and Avoid Difficult Things, and There Is No Spirit of Righteousness and Courage. However, the Westerners' Style of Righteousness Is Very Strong. Not to Mention Other Things, Just Look at Their Righteousness to the Country and the Nation. They Are Extremely Righteous. For the Country, the Nation, and the Society, They Are Willing to Spare No Time and Sacrifice, and They Are Willing to Go Through Fire and Water. Let's Look at the Foreigners in Shanghai Again. They Are Very Helpful in Fighting Fires. The Foreigners in Shanghai Are Actually Far Less Than Those Living in Their Own Country. However, They Still Have Such Righteousness. You Can Imagine the Morality of Their Own People.

Sports News

New Tennis Techniques (50) 222

By J. PARML PARET, Translated by Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun

| All Rights Reserved, Reproduction Prohibited |

Swing the arm backward from the front of the body, and the racket should swing all the way behind the left shoulder. When swinging the racket forward to meet the incoming ball, it should be roughly equal to the height of the waist and slightly in front of the player's standing position. For backhand shots, try to swing forward as far as the right shoulder. When the racket and the ball first come into contact, the player's whole body – from the hips to the chest to the shoulders – should turn forward along with it. After the hitting action is completed, the player's face is almost facing the net. This kind of body rotation increases the power of the shot by adding weight and momentum.

When the incoming ball faces the wrist twist, just like in the forehand shot, the ball must rotate forward. At this time, the string should drag across the ball, and the surface of the ball is brushed, thus producing a rotating motion. This is the special technique of this style, which makes the ball fly forward in a rotating manner, that is, increasing the air pressure above the ball and reducing the air pressure below the ball. Therefore, when the ball flies forward, it has a tendency to fall faster and hits very heavily. The ball still does not fly over the boundary line.

When the backhand topspin is completed, the racket should swing to a place higher than when the shot started. Because this kind of shot, the racket is swinging upward. The time for the racket to contact the ball should be extended as much as possible. After the ball has left the string and flew away, the right arm should swing to the right side as much as possible, using the momentum to the fullest. Because the weight and shoulders are swinging to the right side as much as possible, and the right arm is also stretching straight to the right side as much as possible, the momentum can be fully used up.

When this type of shot is completed, the real position where the racket stops its power varies from player to player according to the momentum of the twisting ball. Some players extremely twist the racket to a level above the horizontal of the right shoulder. There are also very few players who only swing the racket to a position above a semicircle and stop. However, their power to twist the ball is much weaker. This is very obvious.

There is no doubt that the backhand topspin is much more difficult than the forehand topspin. However, some players who specialize in practicing this technique find it easy. Years ago, there was a newly famous player who simply liked to use the backhand to meet the incoming ball. This player's name was Pell T.R. Pell. He invented extremely sophisticated techniques and power for the backhand topspin, and simply using this technique has enabled him to win many leagues many times.

Speaking of the backhand slice or backhand chop, it is much easier than the backhand topspin. The backward swing of the racket is not as far as the topspin, but it should be slightly higher. When shooting forward, the angle is slightly downward, so the contact between the ball and the racket is a sweeping shot from below. Naturally, the racket is lowered more after the shot, and this sweeping shot from below makes the string rub and rotate the ball at the bottom of the ball, so the ball flies forward and dies backward.

Because the racket must pass under the ball, the position where the racket stops after the backhand slice is not only different, but also the angle at which the racket face slopes back is also different.

As for the position where the racket swings after the chop shot is completed, it will be even lower. The difference between the slice and the chop is in the method of spinning the ball differently. When chopping downward, the racket only needs to be slightly angled backward. When shooting, it is diagonally chopped from top to bottom, and the sweeping power is also greater. Therefore, the racket falls even lower. As for the slice, the racket should be angled backward even more, and then hit straight out, but the swing of the shot is less.

The backhand slice is an amazing defensive method. If you can practice it to the same technique as Tilden, it can even be regarded as a dangerous attack method. Because the ball's swing process is shorter, the preparation time for the shot is also less, so the aiming direction to the opponent can be hidden, making it impossible for the opponent to predict. The player can also control the racket more easily. As long as the wrist is slightly changed, the direction of the shot can be changed, which is much more flexible than other shooting techniques.

When the player is forced back by the opponent to the far left corner of the court to meet the incoming ball, the player should use the chop, which can turn danger into safety. If other techniques are used at this time, there will inevitably be mistakes or the power of the return is very weak. When using the backhand topspin again, the player must retreat far behind the shooting position, which is in itself a weakness and not as convenient as the chop.
